<h1>/*Pitjantjatjara Elementary Course and Advanced Course*/||</h1>

<i>/*Developed 1966-68 at the University of Adelaide by Jim Downing, Ken Hale and Gordon Ingkatji.*/||</i> 
<i>/*Audio recorded by Gordon Ingkatji, Henk Siliakus and an unidentified female speaker of Pitjantjatjara.*/||</i> 
<i>/*Gordon Ingkatji's name and voice appear with permission of his family. All efforts have been made to identify and contact the family of the female speaker, but these have so far been unsuccessful.*/||</i> 
<i>/*Multimedia edition formatted by Manny Rayner using the LARA toolkit and corrected by Sasha Wilmoth. View in Chrome or Firefox.*/||</i> 
<b>/*THE PITJANTJATJARA LANGUAGE IS THE PROPERTY OF THE PITJANTJATJARA PEOPLE. ABORIGINAL AND TORRES STRAIT ISLANDER PEOPLE ARE ADVISED THAT THIS SITE CONTAINS VOICES OF DECEASED PERSONS.*/||</n> 

<page><h1>/*Unit 1*/||</h1> 

<h2>/*A. Vocabulary. Listen and repeat.*/||</h2>
nyangatja||
palatja||
nyaratja||
wati||
minyma||
tjitji||
puḻka||
tjukutjuku||
palya||
pikatjara||

<h2>/*B. Now repeat the words and fix the English meanings in your mind.*/||</h2>
nyangatja|| /*<i>this one</i>*/||
palatja|| /*<i>that one near</i>*/||
nyaratja|| /*<i>that one far (or) over there</i>*/||
wati|| /*<i>man</i>*/||
minyma|| /*<i>woman</i>*/||
tjitji|| /*<i>child</i>*/||
puḻka|| /*<i>big</i>*/||
tjukutjuku|| /*<i>small</i>*/||
palya|| /*<i>good or well</i>*/||
pikatjara|| /*<i>sick</i>*/||

<h2>/*C. Listen and repeat the sentences.*/||</h2>
nyangatja palya||
palatja palya||
nyaratja palya||
wati palya||
minyma palya||
tjitji palya||

<h2>/*D. Repeat the sentences and fix the English meanings in your mind.*/||</h2>
nyangatja palya|| /*<i>This one is good (well).</i>*/||
palatja palya|| /*<i>That one near is good (well).</i>*/||
nyaratja palya|| /*<i>That one far is good (well).</i>*/||
wati palya|| /*<i>The man is good (well).</i>*/||
minyma palya|| /*<i>The woman is good (well).</i>*/||
tjitji palya|| /*<i>The child is good (well).</i>*/||

<h2>/*E. Substitution.*/||</h2>
/*<i>You will now·hear a model sentence followed by a cue
Use this cue to make your new sentence. Like this:</i>*/||

/*<i>You will hear:</i>*/|| nyangatja palya|/|palatja||
/*<i>You will say:</i>*/|| palatja palya.||

/*<i>Then you listen for the correct response and repeat
it. This is called a four phase drill, because of
the four items:</i>*/||

/*<i>1. The model:</i>*/|| nyangatja palya|/|palatja||
/*<i>2. Your attempt:</i>*/|| palatja palya||
/*<i>3. The confirmation:</i>*/|| palatja palya||
/*<i>4. Your repetition:</i>*/|| palatja palya||

/*<i>Join in as soon as you understand.</i>*/||

/*<b>First model.</b>*/||
nyangatja palya|/|palatja||
palatja palya|/|nyaratja||
nyaratja palya|/|wati||
wati palya|/|minyma||
minyma palya|/|tjitji||
tjitji palya||

/*<b>Second model.</b>*/||
nyangatja pikatjara|| /*<i>= This one is sick.</i>*/||
nyangatja pikatjara|/|nyaratja||
nyaratja pikatjara|/|palatja||
palatja pikatjara|/|tjitji||
tjitji pikatjara|/|wati||
wati pikatjara|/|minyma||
minyma pikatjara||

/*<b>Third model.</b>*/||
nyangatja tjukutjuku|| /*<i>= This one is small.</i>*/||
nyangatja tjukutjuku|/|palatja||
palatja tjukutjuku|/|nyaratja||
nyaratja tjukutjuku|/|tjitji||
tjitji tjukutjuku|/|minyma||
minyma tjukutjuku|/|wati||
wati tjukutjuku||

/*<b>Fourth model.</b>*/||
nyangatja puḻka|| /*<i>= This one is big.</i>*/||
nyangatja puḻka|/|palatja||
palatja puḻka|/|wati||
wati puḻka|/|minyma||
minyma puḻka|/|tjitji||
tjitji puḻka|/|nyaratja||
nyaratja puḻka||

<h2>/*F. Translation into the language.*/||</h2>
/*<i>You will hear an English statement. Put it into the native language
and listen out for the correct response. Then repeat the correct response.
Off you go.</i>*/||

/*<i>The man is sick.</i>*/|| wati pikatjara.||
/*<i>The child is sick.</i>*/|| tjitji pikatjara.||
/*<i>The child is well.</i>*/|| tjitji palya.||
/*<i>The woman is well.</i>*/|| minyma palya.||
/*<i>The woman is small.</i>*/|| minyma tjukutjuku.||
/*<i>This one is small.</i>*/|| nyangatja tjukutjuku.||
/*<i>This one is big.</i>*/|| nyangatja puḻka.||
/*<i>That one near is big.</i>*/|| palatja puḻka.||
/*<i>That one distant is sick.</i>*/|| nyaratja pikatjara.||
/*<i>That one distant is well.</i>*/|| nyaratja palya.||

/*<b>End of Unit 1</b>*/||

||<page><h1>/*Unit 2*/||</h1>

<h2>/*A. Listen and repeat the following*/||</h2>
wati nyanga||
wati pala||
wati nyara||
minyma nyanga||
minyma pala||
minyma nyara||
tjitji nyanga||
tjitji pala||
tjitji nyara||

<h2>/*B. Now repeat these phrases once again and fix the English meanings in your mind*/||</h2>
wati nyanga|| <i>/*this man*/</i>||
wati pala|| <i>/*that man near*/</i>||
wati nyara|| <i>/*that man far*/</i>||
minyma nyanga|| <i>/*this woman*/</i>||
minyma pala|| <i>/*that woman near*/</i>||
minyma nyara|| <i>/*that woman far*/</i>||
tjitji nyanga|| <i>/*this child*/</i>||
tjitji pala|| <i>/*that child near*/</i>||
tjitji nyara|| <i>/*that child far*/</i>||

<h2>/*C. Listen and repeat the following sentences:*/||</h2>
wati nyanga pikatjara||
wati pala pikatjara||
wati nyara pikatjara||
minyma nyanga palya||
minyma pala palya||
minyma nyara palya||
tjitji nyanga tjukutjuku||
tjitji pala tjukutjuku||
tjitji nyara tjukutjuku||

<h2>/*D. Listen to these sentences once again and fix their English meanings in your mind.*/||</h2>
wati nyanga pikatjara|| <i>/*This man is sick.*/</i>||
wati pala pikatjara|| <i>/*That man near is sick.*/</i>||
wati nyara pikatjara|| <i>/*That man far is sick.*/</i>||
minyma nyanga palya|| <i>/*This woman is well.*/</i>||
minyma pala palya|| <i>/*That woman near is well.*/</i>||
minyma nyara palya|| <i>/*That woman far is well.*/</i>||
tjitji nyanga tjukutjuku|| <i>/*This child is small.*/</i>||
tjitji pala tjukutjuku|| <i>/*That child near is small.*/</i>||
tjitji nyara tjukutjuku|| <i>/*That child far is small.*/</i>||

<h2>/*E.l. Structural Drills. Four phase drill, as you did previously.*/||</h2>
<b>/*First model.*/</b>||
wati nyanga pikatjara|/|wati pala||
wati pala pikatjara|/|wati nyara||
wati nyara pikatjara|/|minyma nyanga||
minyma nyanga pikatjara|/|minyma pala||
minyma pala pikatjara|/|tjitji nyanga||
tjitji nyanga pikatjara|/|tjitji pala||
tjitji pala pikatjara|/|tjitji nyara||
tjitji nyara pikatjara||

<b>/*Second model.*/</b>||
wati nyanga puḻka|/|wati pala||
wati pala puḻka|/|wati nyara||
wati nyara puḻka|/|minyma nyanga||
minyma nyanga puḻka|/|minyma pala||
minyma pala puḻka|/|tjitji nyanga||
tjitji nyanga puḻka|/|tjitji pala||
tjitji pala puḻka|/|tjitji nyara||
tjitji nyara puḻka||

<h2>/*E.2. You are now going to hear a sentence followed by a cue*/||</h2>
<i>/*e.g. well, sick, small, or big. Make up your own statements like this:*/</i>
<i>/*You'll hear:*/</i>|| wati nyanga pikatjara|/|puḻka||
<i>/*You respond:*/</i>|| wati nyanga puḻka||

<i>/*Listen to the correct response, and repeat, etc. Off you go.*/</i>||

<b>/*First model.*/</b>|| 
wati nyanga pikatjara|/|puḻka||
wati nyanga puḻka|/|palya||
wati nyanga palya|/|tjukutjuku||
wati nyanga tjukutjuku||

<b>/*Second model.*/</b>||
minyma pala puḻka|/|pikatjara||
minyma pala pikatjara|/|palya||
minyma pala palya|/|tjukutjuku||
minyma pala tjukutjuku||

<b>/*Third model.*/</b>||
tjitji nyara tjukutjuku|/|pikatjara||
tjitji nyara pikatjara|/|palya||
tjitji nyara palya|/|puḻka||
tjitji nyara puḻka||

<h2>/*E. 3. Mixed Drills*/||</h2>
<i>/*We shall now give you a model, and a cue that may be either
this man, that near child, or the child and so on, or it
can be a word such as well, or sick, or big, or small. It
is up to you to put them in their appropriate place. We'll
start off simply. The confirmation will be given as usual,
please repeat it. Join in as you understand:</i>

<b>Model.</b>*/||
wati puḻka|/|minyma:||
minyma puḻka|/|pikatjara||
minyma pikatjara|/|tjitji pala||
tjitji pala pikatjara|/|tjitji nyanga||
tjitji nyanga pikatjara|/|wati||
wati pikatjara|/|wati nyanga||
wati nyanga pikatjara|/|palya||
wati nyanga palya|/|minyma nyanga||
minyma nyanga palya|/|tjukutjuku||
minyma nyanga tjukutjuku|/|tjitji||
tjitji tjukutjuku|/|palya||
tjitji palya|/|tjitji nyanga||
tjitji nyanga palya|/|puḻka||
tjitji nyanga puḻka||


<h2>/*F. Translate into the language. Four phase drill as before.*/||</h2>
<i>/*The man is sick.*/</i>||  wati pikatjara||
<i>/*This man is sick.*/</i>|| wati nyanga pikatjara||
<i>/*This woman is sick.*/</i>|| minyma nyanga pikatjara||
<i>/*This woman is well.*/</i>|| minyma nyanga palya||
<i>/*The child is well.*/</i>|| tjitji palya||
<i>/*The child is small.*/</i>|| tjitji tjukutjuku||
<i>/*This child is small.*/</i>|| tjitji nyanga tjukutjuku||
<i>/*This child is big.*/</i>|| tjitji nyanga puḻka||
<i>/*That distant man is big.*/</i>|| wati nyara puḻka||
<i>/*That distant woman is big.*/</i>|| minyma nyara puḻka||

/*<b>End of Unit 2</b>*/|| 

||<page><h1>/*Unit 3*/||</h1>

<h2>/*A. Listen and repeat the following pronouns:*/||</h2>
ngayulu||
nyuntu|| 
paluṟu|| 
ngali|| 
nyupali|| 
pula|| 
nganaṉa|| 
nyura|| 
tjana|| 

<h2>/*B. Listen to these words again and fix the English meaning in your mind:*/||</h2>
ngayulu||<i>/* I*/</i>||
nyuntu||<i>/* you*/</i>||
paluṟu||<i>/* he/she/it*/</i>||
ngali||<i>/* we two*/</i>||
nyupali||<i>/* you two*/</i>||
pula||<i>/* they two*/</i>||
nganaṉa||<i>/* we (more than two)*/</i>||
nyura||<i>/* you (more than two)*/</i>||
tjana||<i>/* they (more than two)*/</i>||

<h2>/*C. Listen to the following sentences:*/||</h2>
ngayulu palya||
nyuntu palya||
paluṟu palya||
ngali palya||
nyupali palya||
pula palya||
nganaṉa palya||
nyura palya||
tjana palya||
ngayulu pikatjara||
nyuntu pikatjara||
paluṟu pikatjara||
ngali pikatjara||
nyupali pikatjara||
pula pikatjara||
nganaṉa pikatjara||
nyura pikatjara||
tjana pikatjara||
ngayulu puḻka||
nyuntu puḻka||
paluṟu puḻka||
ngali puḻka||
pula puḻka||
nganaṉa puḻka||
nyura puḻka||
tjana puḻka||
ngayulu tjukutjuku||
nyuntu tjukutjuku||
paluṟu tjukutjuku||
ngali tjukutjuku||
nyupali tjukutjuku||
pula tjukutjuku||
nganaṉa tjukutjuku||
nyura tjukutjuku||
tjana tjukutjuku||

<h2>/*D. Listen to the following sentences, repeat them and
fix the English in your mind.*/||</h2>
ngayulu palya||<i>/* I am well.*/</i>||
nyuntu pikatjara||<i>/* You are sick.*/</i>||
paluṟu pikatjara||<i>/* He/she, it is sick.*/</i>||
ngali palya||<i>/* We two are well.*/</i>||
nyupali pikatjara||<i>/* You two are sick.*/</i>||
pula puḻka||<i>/* They two are big.*/</i>||
nganaṉa puḻka||<i>/* We are big.*/</i>||
nyura tjukutjuku||<i>/* You are small. (more than two)*/</i>||
tjana tjukutjuku||<i>/* They are small. (more than two)*/</i>||

<h2>/*E. Drills. Substitutions. You'll hear a model followed by a cue. Use the cue to make a new sentence. For instance:*/||</h2>
<i>/*You'll hear:*/</i>|| ngayulu palya|/|pikatjara||
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| ngayulu pikatjara||
<i>/*Join in as soon as you understand.</i>
<b>First model.</b>*/||
ngayulu palya|/|pikatjara||
ngayulu pikatjara|/|puḻka||
ngayulu puḻka|/|tjukutjuku||
ngayulu tjukutjuku|/|nyuntu||
nyuntu tjukutjuku|/|paluṟu||
paluṟu tjukutjuku|/|ngali||
ngali tjukutjuku|/|nyupali||
nyupali tjukutjuku|/|puḻka||
nyupali puḻka|/|pikatjara||
nyupali pikatjara|/|palya||
nyupali palya|/|pula||
pula palya|/|nganaṉa||
nganaṉa palya|/|nyura||
nyura palya|/|tjana||
tjana palya||

/*<b>Drill 2.</b><i> You'll now hear a sentence in the "I" form</i>*/|| (ngayulu).||
<i>/*Change these to the "you" form</i>*/|| (nyuntu);||/*<i> listen for
the correct response and repeat it.</i>*/||

/*<b>First model.</b>*/||
ngayulu palya|/|nyuntu palya||
ngayulu pikatjara|/|nyuntu pikatjara||
ngayulu puḻka|/|nyuntu puḻka||
ngayulu tjukutjuku|/|nyuntu tjukutjuku||

/*<b>Second model.</b>*/||
/*<i>Now change to the "he" form (the</i>*/|| paluṟu||/*<i> form).</i>*/||
ngayulu puḻka|/|paluṟu puḻka||
ngayulu pikatjara|/|paluṟu pikatjara||
ngayulu palya|/|paluṟu palya||
ngayulu tjukutjuku|/|paluṟu tjukutjuku||

/*<b>Third model.</b>*/||
/*<i>Now change from the "he" form</i>*//|| (paluṟu)||/*<i> to the
"dual we" form (the</i>*/|| ngali||/*<i> form).*/||/* Off you go.</i>*/||
paluṟu puḻka|/|ngali puḻka||
paluṟu tjukutjuku|/|ngali tjukutjuku||
paluṟu palya|/|ngali palya||
paluṟu pikatjara|/|ngali pikatjara||

/*<b>Fourth model.</b><i> Now change from the "we" form (the</i>*/|| ngali||/*<i> form) to the
dual "you two" form</i>*/|| (nyupali).||/*<i> Off you go.</i>*/||
ngali puḻka|/|nyupali puḻka||
ngali palya|/|nyupali palya||
ngali tjukutjuku|/|nyupali tjukutjuku||
ngali pikatjara|/|nyupali pikatjara||

/*<b>Fifth model.</b> <i>Now change from the "I" form (the</i>*/|| ngayulu)||/*<i> to the
"we" form</i>*/|| (nganaṉa).||/*<i> Off you go.</i>*/||
ngayulu tjukutjuku|/|nganaṉa tjukutjuku||
ngayulu palya|/|nganaṉa palya||
ngayulu pikatjara|/|nganaṉa pikatjara||
ngayulu puḻka|/|nganaṉa puḻka||

<h2>/*F. Translation into the language. Four phase drill as usual.*/||</h2>
/*<i>I am well.</i>*/|| ngayulu palya||
/*<i>He is well.</i>*/|| paluṟu palya||
/*<i>The man is well.</i>*/|| wati palya||
/*<i>The child is well.</i>*/|| tjitji palya||
/*<i>The child is sick.</i>*/|| tjitji pikatjara||
/*<i>It is sick.</i>*/|| paluṟu pikatjara||
/*<i>You (singular) are sick.</i>*/|| nyuntu pikatjara||
/*<i>You (plural) are sick.</i>*/|| nyura pikatjara||
/*<i>You (plural) are big.</i>*/|| nyura puḻka||
/*<i>I am big.</i>*/|| ngayulu puḻka||
/*<i>This one is big.</i>*/|| nyangatja puḻka||
/*<i>We two are big.</i>*/|| ngali puḻka||
/*<i>We two are small.</i>*/|| ngali tjukutjuku||
/*<i>They two are small.</i>*/|| pula tjukutjuku||
/*<i>We are small.</i>*/|| nganaṉa tjukutjuku||
/*<i>You two are small.</i>*/|| nyupali tjukutjuku||
/*<i>They (plural) are small.</i>*/|| tjana tjukutjuku||
<b>/*End of Unit 3*/</b>||

||<page><h1>/*Unit 4*/||</h1>
<h2>/*A. Vocabulary. Listen and repeat*/||</h2>
nyanganpa||
palanpa||
nyaranpa||
paku||
pukuḻpa||
waṟa||
muṯumuṯu||
aṉangu||
papa||
maḻu||

<h2>/*B. Repeat and fix the English meanings in your mind*/||</h2>
nyanganpa||<i>/*  these*/</i>||
palanpa||<i>/* those near, more than two*/</i>||
nyaranpa||<i>/* those far, more than two*/</i>||
paku||<i>/* tired*/</i>||
pukuḻpa||<i>/* happy*/</i>||
waṟa||<i>/* tall or long*/</i>||
muṯumuṯu||<i>/*  short*/</i>||
aṉangu||<i>/* person*/</i>||
papa||<i>/* dog*/</i>||
maḻu||<i>/* kangaroo*/</i>||

<h2>/*C. Repeat the following phrases*/||</h2>
wati nyanganpa||
minyma nyanganpa||
tjitji nyanganpa||
aṉangu nyanganpa||
papa nyanganpa||
maḻu nyanganpa||
tjitji palanpa||
wati palanpa||
minyma nyaranpa||
aṉangu nyaranpa||
wati paku||
tjitji pukuḻpa||
aṉangu waṟa||
minyma muṯumuṯu||
minyma paku||
wati pukuḻpa||
papa tjukutjuku||
maḻu puḻka||
wati nyanga pukuḻpa||
wati nyanganpa pukuḻpa||
maḻu pala puḻka||
maḻu palanpa puḻka||
minyma nyara pikatjara||
minyma nyaranpa pikatjara||
ngayulu paku||
nyuntu paku||
paluṟu paku||
ngayulu pukuḻpa||
nyuntu pukuḻpa||
paluṟu pukuḻpa||
ngali waṟa||
nyupali waṟa||
pula waṟa||
nganaṉa paku||
nyura paku||
tjana paku||
ngayulu muṯumuṯu||
nyuntu muṯumuṯu||
paluṟu muṯumuṯu||
nyangatja paku||
nyanganpa paku||
palatja waṟa||
palanpa waṟa||
nyaratja pukuḻpa||
nyaranpa pukuḻpa||

<h2>/*D. English meanings*/||</h2>
wati nyanganpa||<i>/*  these men*/</i>||
minyma nyanganpa||<i>/*  these women*/</i>||
tjitji nyanganpa||<i>/*  these children*/</i>||
aṉangu nyanganpa||<i>/*  these persons (people)*/</i>||
papa nyanganpa||<i>/*  these dogs*/</i>||
maḻu nyanganpa||<i>/*  these kangaroos*/</i>||
tjitji palanpa||<i>/*  those near children*/</i>||
wati palanpa||<i>/*  those near men*/</i>||
minyma nyaranpa||<i>/*  those distant women*/</i>||
aṉangu nyaranpa||<i>/*  those distant people*/</i>||
wati paku||<i>/*  the man is tired*/</i>||
tjitji pukuḻpa||<i>/*  the child is happy*/</i>||
aṉangu waṟa||<i>/*  the person is tall*/</i>||
minyma muṯumuṯu||<i>/*  the woman is short*/</i>||
minyma paku||<i>/*  the woman is tired*/</i>||
wati pukuḻpa||<i>/*  the man is happy*/</i>||
papa tjukutjuku||<i>/*  the dog is small*/</i>||
maḻu puḻka||<i>/*  the kangaroo is big*/</i>||
wati nyanga pukuḻpa||<i>/*  this man is happy*/</i>||
maḻu pala puḻka||<i>/*  that near kangaroo is big*/</i>||
maḻu palanpa puḻka||<i>/*  those near kangaroos are big*/</i>||
minyma nyara pikatjara||<i>/*  that far woman is sick*/</i>||
minyma nyaranpa pikatjara||<i>/*  those far women are sick*/</i>||
ngayulu paku||<i>/*  I am tired*/</i>||
nyuntu paku||<i>/*  you are tired*/</i>||
paluṟu paku||<i>/*  he/she/it is tired*/</i>||
ngayulu pukuḻpa||<i>/*  I am happy*/</i>||
nyuntu pukuḻpa||<i>/*  you are happy ·*/</i>||
paluṟu pukuḻpa||<i>/*  he/she/it is happy*/</i>||
ngali waṟa||<i>/*  we two are tall*/</i>||
nyupali waṟa||<i>/*  you two are tall*/</i>||
pula waṟa||<i>/*  they two are tall*/</i>||
nganaṉa paku||<i>/*  we are tired*/</i>||
nyura paku||<i>/*  you are tired*/</i>||
tjana paku||<i>/*  they are tired*/</i>||
ngayulu muṯumuṯu||<i>/*  I am short*/</i>||
nyuntu muṯumuṯu||<i>/*  you are short*/</i>||
paluṟu muṯumuṯu||<i>/*  he/she/it is short*/</i>||
nyangatja paku||<i>/*  this one is tired*/</i>||
nyanganpa paku||<i>/*  these ones are tired*/</i>||
palatja waṟa||<i>/*  that near one is tall*/</i>||
palanpa waṟa||<i>/*  those near ones are tall*/</i>||
nyaratja pukuḻpa||<i>/*  that far one is happy*/</i>||
nyaranpa pukuḻpa||<i>/*  those far ones are happy*/</i>||

<h2>/*E. Substitutions: Four phase drill*/||</h2>
<b>/*First model.*/</b>||
wati puḻka|/|paku||
wati paku|/|pukuḻpa||
wati pukuḻpa|/|waṟa||
wati waṟa|/|muṯumuṯu||
wati muṯumuṯu|/|minyma||
minyma muṯumuṯu|/|tjitji||
tjitji muṯumuṯu|/|aṉangu||
aṉangu muṯumuṯu|/|puḻka||
aṉangu puḻka|/|papa||
papa puḻka|/|maḻu||
maḻu puḻka|/|paku||
maḻu paku|/|papa||
papa paku||

<b>/*Second model.*/</b>||
<i>/*Conversion from singular to plural, demonstrative,
You are asked to change from "this" to "these".
Like this:*/</i>||
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| nyangatja puḻka|/|nyanganpa|| 
<i>/*You'll say:*/</i>|| nyanganpa puḻka||
<i>/*Listen for the correct response and repeat it.
Off you go.*/</i>||

nyangatja puḻka|/|nyanganpa||
nyanganpa puḻka||
palatja puḻka|/|palanpa||
palanpa puḻka||
nyaratja puḻka|/|nyaranpa||
nyaranpa puḻka||
wati nyanga puḻka|/|wati nyanganpa||
wati nyanganpa puḻka||
tjitji pala tjukutjuku|/|tjitji palanpa||

tjitji palanpa tjukutjuku||
maḻu nyara puḻka|/|maḻu nyaranpa||
maḻu nyaranpa puḻka||
minyma nyanga pikatjara|/|minyma nyanganpa||
minyma nyanganpa pikatjara||
aṉangu pala pukuḻpa|/|aṉangu palanpa||
aṉangu palanpa pukuḻpa||
papa nyara paku|/|papa nyaranpa||
papa nyaranpa paku||

<b>/*Third model.*/</b>||
<i>/*This is a drill in which you will be given a
cue that may be either "this", "this man", "I",
"those men" , "the man", and so on; or it may be
a change from "is tired" to "is tall" and so on.
Have fun!*/</i>||
wati puḻka|/|ngayulu||
ngayulu puḻka|/|pikatjara||
ngayulu pikatjara|/|minyma pala||
minyma pala pikatjara|/|minyma palanpa||
minyma palanpa pikatjara|/|paku||
minyma palanpa paku|/|maḻu||
maḻu paku|/|papa||
papa paku|/|tjukutjuku||
papa tjukutjuku|/|aṉangu||
aṉangu tjukutjuku|/|muṯumuṯu||
aṉangu muṯumuṯu|/|aṉangu nyara||
aṉangu nyara muṯumuṯu|/|nyuntu||
nyuntu muṯumuṯu|/|waṟa||
nyuntu waṟa|/|nganaṉa||
nganaṉa waṟa|/|pukuḻpa||
nganaṉa pukuḻpa||

<h2>/*F. Translate into the language*/||</h2>
<i>/*The man is sick.*/</i>||  wati pikatjara||
<i>/*The child is happy.*/</i>||  tjitji pukuḻpa||
<i>/*The person is tall.*/</i>||  aṉangu waṟa||
<i>/*The woman is short.*/</i>||  minyma muṯumuṯu||
<i>/*The dog is small.*/</i>||  papa tjukutjuku||
<i>/*The kangaroo is big.*/</i>||  maḻu puḻka||
<i>/*This person is tired.*/</i>||  aṉangu nyanga paku||
<i>/*These women are happy.*/</i>||  minyma nyanganpa pukuḻpa||
<i>/*I am tired.*/</i>||  ngayulu paku||
<i>/*We are happy.*/</i>||  nganaṉa pukuḻpa||
<i>/*That near dog is big.*/</i>||  papa pala puḻka||
<i>/*That far kangaroo is tired.*/</i>||  maḻu nyara paku||
<i>/*Those far children are happy.*/</i>||  tjitji nyaranpa tjukutjuku||
<i>/*You two are happy.*/</i>||  nyupali pukuḻpa||
<i>/*We two are well.*/</i>||  ngali palya||
/*<b>End of Unit 4</b>*/||

||<page><h1>/*Unit 5*/||</h1>
<h2>/*A. Vocabulary. Listen and repeat:*/||</h2>
uwa||
wiya||

<h2>/*B. With English meanings:*/||</h2>
uwa|| <i>/* yes*/</i>||
wiya|| <i>/* no*/</i>||

<h2>/*C. Repeat the following phrases and sentences:*/||</h2>
nyuntu palya?|| uwa, ngayulu palya.||
nyuntu paku?|| uwa, ngayulu paku.||
nyuntu pukuḻpa?|| uwa, ngayulu pukuḻpa.||
nyupali palya?|| uwa, ngali palya.||
nyupali paku?|| uwa, ngali paku.||
nyupali pukuḻpa?|| uwa, ngali pukuḻpa.||
nyura palya?|| uwa, nganaṉa palya.||
nyura paku?|| uwa, nganaṉa paku.||
nyura pukuḻpa?|| uwa, nganaṉa pukuḻpa.||
tjitji nyanga palya?|| uwa, paluṟu palya.||
tjitji nyanga paku?|| uwa, paluṟu paku.||
tjitji nyanga pukuḻpa?|| uwa, paluṟu pukuḻpa.||
nyuntu pikatjara?|| wiya, ngayulu palya.||
nyuntu pikatjara?|| wiya, ngayulu pikatjara|wiya.||
nyuntu paku?|| wiya, ngayulu paku|wiya.||
nyuntu pukuḻpa?|| wiya, ngayulu pukuḻpa|wiya.||
nyupali pikatjara?|| wiya, ngali palya.||
nyupali pikatjara?|| wiya, ngali pikatjara|wiya.||
nyupali paku?|| wiya, ngali paku|wiya.||
nyupali pukuḻpa?|| wiya, ngali pukuḻpa|wiya.||
tjitji pikatjara?|| wiya, tjitji palya.||
tjitji pikatjara?|| wiya, tjitji pikatjara|wiya.||
wati paku?|| wiya, wati paku|wiya.||
minyma pukuḻpa?|| wiya, minyma pukuḻpa|wiya.||
wati nyanga pikatjara?|| wiya, paluṟu palya.||
wati nyanga pikatjara?|| wiya, paluṟu pikatjara|wiya.||
tjitji pala paku?|| wiya, paluṟu paku|wiya.||
minyma nyara pukuḻpa?|| wiya, paluṟu pukuḻpa|wiya.||

<h2>/*D. Repeat and fix the English meanings in your mind*/||</h2>
nyuntu palya?|| uwa, ngayulu palya.|| <i>/*Are you well? Yes. I am well.*/</i>||
nyuntu paku?|| uwa, ngayulu paku.|| <i>/*Are you tired? Yes, I am tired.*/</i>||
nyuntu pukuḻpa?|| uwa, ngayulu pukuḻpa.|| <i>/*Are you happy? Yes, I am happy.*/</i>||
nyupali palya?|| uwa, ngali palya.|| <i>/*Are you two well? Yes, we are well.*/</i>||
nyupali paku?|| uwa, ngali paku.|| <i>/*Are you two tired? Yes, we are tired.*/</i>||
nyupali pukuḻpa?|| uwa, ngali pukuḻpa.|| <i>/*Are you two happy? Yes we are happy.*/</i>||
nyura palya?|| uwa, nganaṉa palya.|| <i>/*Are you well? Yes, we are well.*/</i>||
nyura paku?|| uwa, nganaṉa paku.|| <i>/*Are you tired? Yes, we are tired.*/</i>||
nyura pukuḻpa?|| uwa, nganaṉa pukuḻpa.|| <i>/*Are you happy? Yes, we are happy.*/</i>||
tjitji nyanga palya?|| uwa, paluṟu palya.|| <i>/*Is this child well? Yes, it is well.*/</i>||
tjitji nyanga paku?|| uwa, paluṟu paku.|| <i>/*Is this child tired? Yes, it is tired.*/</i>||
tjitji nyanga pukuḻpa?|| uwa, paluṟu pukuḻpa.|| <i>/*Is this child happy? Yes, it is happy.*/</i>||
nyuntu pikatjara?|| wiya, ngayulu palya.|| <i>/*Are you sick? No, I am well.*/</i>||
nyuntu pikatjara?|| wiya, ngayulu pikatjara|wiya.|| <i>/*Are you sick? No, I am not sick.*/</i>||
nyuntu paku?|| wiya, ngayulu paku|wiya.|| <i>/*Are you tired? No, I am not tired.*/</i>||
nyuntu pukuḻpa?|| wiya, ngayulu pukuḻpa|wiya.|| <i>/*Are you happy? No, I am not happy.*/</i>||
nyupali pikatjara?|| wiya, ngali palya.|| <i>/*Are you two sick? No, we are well.*/</i>||
nyupali pikatjara?|| wiya, ngali pikatjara|wiya.|| <i>/*Are you two sick? No, we are not sick.*/</i>||
nyupali paku?|| wiya, ngali paku|wiya.|| <i>/*Are you two tired? No, we are not tired.*/</i>||
nyupali pukuḻpa?|| wiya, ngali pukuḻpa|wiya.|| <i>/*Are you two happy? No, we are not happy.*/</i>||
tjitji pikatjara?|| wiya, tjitji palya.|| <i>/*Is the child sick? No, the child is well.*/</i>||
tjitji pikatjara?|| wiya, tjitji pikatjara|wiya.|| <i>/*Is the child sick? No, the child is not sick.*/</i>||
wati paku?|| wiya, wati paku|wiya.|| <i>/*Is the man tired? No, the man is not tired.*/</i>||
minyma pukuḻpa?|| wiya, minyma pukuḻpa|wiya.|| <i>/*Is the woman happy? No, the woman is not happy.*/</i>||
wati nyanga pikatjara?|| wiya, paluṟu palya.|| <i>/*Is this man sick? No, he is well.*/</i>||
wati nyanga pikatjara?|| wiya, paluṟu pikatjara|wiya.|| <i>/*Is this man sick? No, he is not sick.*/</i>||
tjitji pala paku?|| wiya, paluṟu paku|wiya.|| <i>/*Is that (near) child tired? No, it is not tired.*/</i>||
minyma nyara pukuḻpa?|| wiya, paluṟu pukuḻpa|wiya.|| <i>/*Is that (far) woman happy? No, she is not happy.*/</i>|| 

<h2>/*E. Drills You will hear a question in the language. Answer in the affirmative, like this:*/||</h2>
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| nyuntu palya?||
<i>/*You answer:*/</i>|| uwa, ngayulu palya||
<i>/*Four phase drill as usual.*/</i>||
nyuntu palya?|| uwa, ngayulu palya.||
nyuntu pikatjara?|| uwa, ngayulu pikatjara.||
nyuntu pukuḻpa?|| uwa, ngayulu pukuḻpa.||
nyuntu paku?|| uwa, ngayulu paku.||
nyupali pikatjara?|| uwa, ngali pikatjara.||
nyupali pukuḻpa?|| uwa, ngali pukuḻpa.||
nyura palya?|| uwa, nganaṉa palya.||
nyura pikatjara?|| uwa, nganaṉa pikatjara.||
tjitji nyanga pikatjara?|| uwa, paluṟu pikatjara.||
wati nyanga paku?|| uwa, paluṟu paku.||

<i>/*Now answer similar questions in the negative, using wiya.*/</i>||
nyuntu pikatjara?|| wiya, ngayulu pikatjara|wiya|| <i>/*or*/</i> ||wiya, ngayulu palya.||
nyupali pikatjara?|| wiya, ngali pikatjara|wiya|| <i>/*or*/</i>|| wiya, ngali palya.||
nyupali paku?|| wiya, ngali paku|wiya.||
nyura paku?|| wiya, nganaṉa paku|wiya.||
tjitji nyara paku?|| wiya, paluṟu paku|wiya.||
minyma nyara paku?|| wiya, paluṟu paku|wiya.||
maḻu nyara puḻka?|| wiya, paluṟu tjukutjuku.||
tjitji nyara waṟa?|| wiya, paluṟu muṯumuṯu.||

<h2>/*F. Translate into the Language. Four phase drill.*/||</h2>
<i>/*Are you (singular) well?*/</i>|| nyuntu palya?||
<i>/*Yes, I am well.*/</i>|| uwa, ngayulu palya.||
<i>/*Are you two tired?*/</i>|| nyupali paku?||
<i>/*No, we are not tired.*/</i>|| wiya, ngali paku|wiya.||
<i>/*Is the child tall?*/</i>|| tjitji waṟa?||
<i>/*No, the child is short.*/</i>|| wiya, tjitji muṯumuṯu.||
<i>/*Are they (plural) sick?*/</i>|| tjana pikatjara?||
<i>/*Yes, they are sick.*/</i>|| uwa, tjana pikatjara.||
<i>/*Is the kangaroo sick?*/</i>|| maḻu pikatjara?||
<i>/*No, the kangaroo is well.*/</i>|| wiya, maḻu palya.||
<i>/*Are you all tired?*/</i>|| nyura paku?||
<i>/*Yes, we are all tired.*/</i>|| uwa, nganaṉa paku.||
<i>/*End of Unit 5*/</i>||

||<page><h1>/*Unit 6*/||</h1>
<h2>/*A. Vocabulary. Listen and repeat:*/||</h2>
palya|ṉa#ngayulu#||
palya|n#nyuntu#||
palya||
palya|li#ngali#||
palya|la#nganaṉa#||
palya|ya#tjana#||
paku|ṉa#ngayulu#||
paku|n#nyuntu#||
paku||
paku|li#ngali#||
paku|la#nganaṉa#||
paku|ya#tjana#||

<h2>/*B. Now repeat these again and learn their English meanings:*/||</h2>
palya|ṉa#ngayulu#|| <i>/*I am well*/</i>||
palya|n#nyuntu#|| <i>/*you (singular) are well*/</i>||
palya|| <i>/*he, she, it is well*/</i>||
palya|li#ngali#|| <i>/*we (two) are well*/</i>||
palya|la#nganaṉa#|| <i>/*we (plural) are well*/</i>||
palya|ya#tjana#|| <i>/*they (plural) are well*/</i>||
paku|ṉa#ngayulu#|| <i>/*I am tired*/</i>||
paku|n#nyuntu#|| <i>/*you are tired*/</i>||
paku|| <i>/*he, she, it is tired*/</i>||
paku|li#ngali#|| <i>/*we two are tired*/</i>||
paku|la#nganaṉa#|| <i>/*we all are tired*/</i>||
paku|ya#tjana#|| <i>/*they all are tired*/</i>||

<h2>/*C. What you have just heard are the so-called short forms of sentences such as:*/||</h2>
ngayulu palya|| <i>/*meaning I am well*/</i>||
ngayulu paku|| <i>/*meaning I am tired and so on*/</i>||
<i>/*You will have noticed there are no forms of sentences such as:*/</i>||
nyupali palya|| <i>/*you two are well*/</i>||
pula palya|| <i>/*they two are well*/</i>||
nyura palya|| <i>/*you (plural) are well*/</i>||
<i>/*In other words, these are suffixed forms of the pronouns:*/</i>||
ngayulu|| <i>/*I*/</i>||
nyuntu|| <i>/*you*/</i>||
paluṟu|| <i>/*he, she, it*/</i>||
ngali|| <i>/*we two*/</i>||
nganaṉa|| <i>/*we all*/</i>||
tjana|| <i>/*they all*/</i>||
<i>/*But there are no such forms for:*/</i>||
nyupali|| <i>/*you two*/</i>||
pula|| <i>/*they two*/</i>||
nyura|| <i>/*you all*/</i>||

<i>/*You will have noticed that the ending corresponding
to*/</i>|| paluṟu|| <i>/*is a zero*/</i>|| paluṟu palya|| <i>/*simply
corresponds to short form*/</i>|| palya.||
<i>/*Now listen to the following sentences and repeat them:*/</i>||
palya|ṉa#ngayulu#||
paku|ṉa#ngayulu#||
pukuḻpa|ṉa#ngayulu#||
pikatjara|ṉa#ngayulu#||
waṟa|ṉa#ngayulu#||
muṯumuṯu|ṉa#ngayulu#||
tjukutjuku|ṉa#ngayulu#||
puḻka|ṉa#ngayulu#||
palya|n#nyuntu#||
pikatjara|n#nyuntu#||
paku||
pukuḻpa||
pikatjara|li#ngali#||
paku|li#ngali#||
pikatjara|la#nganaṉa#||
paku|la#nganaṉa#||
pikatjara|ya#tjana#||
pukuḻpa|ya#tjana#||

<h2>/*D. Repeat the sentences you've just heard, and fix the English meanings in your mind.*/||</h2>
palya|ṉa#ngayulu#|| <i>/*I am well*/</i>||
paku|ṉa#ngayulu#|| <i>/*I am tired*/</i>||

tjukutjuku|ṉa#ngayulu#|| <i>/*I am small*/</i>||
puḻka|ṉa#ngayulu#|| <i>/*I am big*/</i>||

pikatjara|n#nyuntu#|| <i>/*you are sick*/</i>||
paku|| <i>/*he is tired*/</i>||
pukuḻpa|| <i>/*he is happy*/</i>||
pikatjara|li#ngali# ||<i>/*we two are sick*/</i>||

pukuḻpa|ya#tjana#|| <i>/*they all are happy*/</i>||

<h2>/*E. Drills*/||</h2>

<i>/*Join in when you understand.*/</i>||
ngayulu palya|| palya|ṉa#ngayulu#||
ngayulu pukuḻpa||  pukuḻpa|ṉa#ngayulu#||

ngali pikatjara|| pikatjara|li#ngali#||
ngali tjukutjuku|| tjukutjuku|li#ngali#||
nganaṉa paku|| paku|la#nganaṉa#||
nganaṉa palya|| palya|la#nganaṉa#||
tjana paku|| paku|ya#tjana#||
tjana pikatjara|| pikatjara|ya#tjana#||
<i>/*Model 2. We shall now ask you a question in the long form.
Reply in the affirmative, using the short form. Like this:*/</i>||
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| nyuntu palya?||
<i>/*You will say:*/</i>|| uwa, palya|ṉa#ngayulu#.||
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||
nyuntu palya?|| uwa, palya|ṉa#ngayulu#||
nyuntu paku?|| uwa, paku|ṉa#ngayulu#||
nyuntu pikatjara?|| uwa, pikatjara|ṉa#ngayulu#||
nyupali pikatjara?||  uwa, pikatjara|li#ngali#||

nyura paku?|| uwa, paku|la#nganaṉa#||
nyura pikatjara?|| uwa, pikatjara|la#nganaṉa#||
paluṟu pikatjara?|| uwa, pikatjara||
paluṟu paku?|| uwa, paku||
paluṟu muṯumuṯu?|| uwa, muṯumuṯu||
paluṟu pukuḻpa?|| uwa, pukuḻpa||
tjana pukuḻpa?||  uwa, pukuḻpa|ya#tjana#||
tjana paku?|| uwa, paku|ya#tjana#||
tjana tjukutjuku|| uwa, tjukutjuku|ya#tjana#||

<h2>/*F. Translate into Pitjantjatjara using short forms where possible.
Four phase drill, as usual.*/||</h1>
<i>/*I am well*/</i>|| palya|ṉa#ngayulu#||
<i>/*you are sick*/</i>|| pikatjara|n#nyuntu#||
<i>/*you two are tired*/</i>|| nyupali paku||
<i>/*you all are big*/</i>|| nyura puḻka||
<i>/*he is small*/</i>|| tjukutjuku||
<i>/*they are short*/</i>|| muṯumuṯu|ya#tjana#||
<i>/*we two are small*/</i>|| tjukutjuku|li#ngali#||
<i>/*they are tired*/</i>|| paku|ya#tjana#||
<i>/*we all are happy*/</i>|| pukuḻpa|la#nganaṉa#||
<i>/*I am big*/</i>|| puḻka|ṉa#ngayulu#||
<i>/*she is sick*/</i>|| pikatjara||
<i>/*I am happy*/</i>|| pukuḻpa|ṉa#ngayulu#||

<i>/*End of Unit 6*/</i>|| 

||<page><h1>/*Unit 7*/||</h1>
<h2>/*A. Vocabulary. Listen and repeat:*/||</h2>
nguḻu||
rapa||
ngananya||
nyaa||

<h2>/*B. Vocabulary and English meanings. Learn them side by side.*/||</h2>
nguḻu||  <i>/*afraid, frightened*/</i>||
rapa||  <i>/*unafraid, confident*/</i>||
ngananya||  <i>/*who?*/</i>||
nyaa||  <i>/*what?*/</i>||

<h2>/*C. Listen to these sentences and repeat them.*/||</h2>
ngananya paku?||   ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku||
ngananya pikatjara?||  ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# pikatjara||
ngananya nguḻu?||  ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# nguḻu||
ngananya rapa?||  ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# rapa||
ngananya paku?||  tjitji nyanga paku||
ngananya pikatjara?||  tjitji nyara pikatjara||
ngananya nguḻu?||  ngali|li#ngali# nguḻu||
ngananya paku?||  nganaṉa|la#nganaṉa# paku||
nyuntu|n#nyuntu# paku?||  uwa, paku|ṉa#ngayulu#||
nyuntu|n#nyuntu# pikatjara?||  uwa, pikatjara|ṉa#ngayulu#||
nyuntu|n#nyuntu# nguḻu?||  uwa, nguḻu|ṉa#ngayulu#||
nyaa puḻka?||  maḻu puḻka||
nyaa tjukutjuku?||  papa tjukutjuku||
nyaa nyangatja?||  nyangatja maḻu||
nyaa palatja?||  palatja papa||

<h2>/*D. Listen once more to these dialogue sentences.*/||</h2>
<i>/*Repeat them and fix their English meanings in your mind.*/</i>||

ngananya paku?||   <i>/*Who is tired?*/</i>||
ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku||   <i>/*I am tired.*/</i>||
ngananya pikatjara?||   <i>/*Who is sick?*/</i>||
ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# pikatjara||   <i>/*I am sick.*/</i> ||
ngananya nguḻu?||   <i>/*Who is afraid?*/</i>||
ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# nguḻu||  <i>/*I am afraid.*/</i>||
ngananya rapa?||   <i>/*Who is unafraid?*/</i>||
ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# rapa||   <i>/*I am unafraid.*/</i>||
ngananya paku?||   <i>/*Who is tired?*/</i>||
tjitji nyanga paku||   <i>/*This child is tired.*/</i>||
ngananya pikatjara?||   <i>/*Who is sick?*/</i>||
tjitji nyara pikatjara||   <i>/*That far child is sick.*/</i>||
ngananya nguḻu?||   <i>/*Who is afraid?*/</i>||
ngali|li#ngali# nguḻu||  <i>/*We two are afraid.*/</i>||
ngananya paku?||  <i>/*Who is tired?*/</i>||
nganaṉa|la#nganaṉa# paku||   <i>/*We all are tired.*/</i>||
nyuntu|n#nyuntu# paku?||   <i>/*Are you tired?*/</i>||
uwa, paku|ṉa#ngayulu#||   <i>/*Yes, I am tired.*/</i>||
nyuntu|n#nyuntu# pikatjara?||   <i>/*Are you sick?*/</i>||
uwa, pikatjara|ṉa#ngayulu#||   <i>/*Yes, I am sick.*/</i>||
nyuntu|n#nyuntu# nguḻu?||   <i>/*Are you afraid?*/</i>||
uwa, nguḻu|ṉa#ngayulu#||   <i>/*Yes, I am afraid.*/</i>||
nyaa puḻka?||   <i>/*What is big?*/</i>||
maḻu puḻka||   <i>/*The kangaroo is big.*/</i>||
nyaa tjukutjuku?||  <i>/*What is small?*/</i>||
papa tjukutjuku||   <i>/*The dog is small.*/</i>||
nyaa nyangatja?||  <i>/*What is this?*/</i>||
nyangatja maḻu||   <i>/*This is a kangaroo.*/</i>||
nyaa palatja?||  <i>/*What is that near?*/</i>||
palatja papa||   <i>/*That near is a dog.*/</i>||

<h2>/*E. Drills.*/||</h2>

<i>/*Model 1. Substitution. Use the cue to make a new sentence.*/</i>||
<i>/*Four phase drill. Off you go.*/</i>||

wati puḻka||  nguḻu||
wati nguḻu||  paku||
wati paku||  rapa||
wati rapa||  tjitji||
tjitji rapa||  minyma||
minyma rapa||  pikatjara||
minyma pikatjara||  nguḻu||
minyma nguḻu||  maḻu||
maḻu nguḻu||  ngayulu||
ngayulu nguḻu|| rapa||
ngayulu rapa||  nyuntu||
nyuntu rapa||  paluṟu||
paluṟu rapa||  paku||
paluṟu paku||  ngali||
ngali paku||  tjana||
tjana paku||  puḻka||
tjana puḻka||  nganaṉa||
nganaṉa puḻka||

<i>/*Model 2.*/</i>||

<i>/*You'll hear a sentence in the pronoun form:*/</i>||
<i>/*restate it using the pronoun together with the personal ending.*/</i>||
<i>/*Like this:*/</i>||

<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| ngayulu palya||
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# palya||

<i>/*another example:*/</i>||
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| nyuntu paku||
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| nyuntu|n#nyuntu# paku||
<i>/*Listen for the correct response and repeat it. Off you go.*/</i>||

ngayulu palya||  ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# palya||
nyuntu paku||  nyuntu|n#nyuntu# paku||
paluṟu paku||  paluṟu paku||
ngali pikatjara||  ngali|li#ngali# pikatjara||
nganaṉa tjukutjuku||  nganaṉa|la#nganaṉa# tjukutjuku||
tjana puḻka||  tjana|ya#tjana# puḻka||
ngayulu pukuḻpa||  ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# pukuḻpa||
paluṟu muṯumuṯu||  paluṟu muṯumuṯu||
nganaṉa waṟa||  nganaṉa|la#nganaṉa# waṟa||
nyuntu rapa||  nyuntu|n#nyuntu# rapa||
ngali nguḻu||  ngali|li#ngali# nguḻu||
nyuntu pikatjara||  nyuntu|n#nyuntu# pikatjara||

<i>/*You have now learned three ways of saying "I am tired"
and such sentences.*/</i>||

<i>/*First single pronoun form:*/</i>||  ngayulu paku||
<i>/*Second short form:*/</i>||  paku|ṉa#ngayulu#||
<i>/*Third empatic form:*/</i>||  ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku||

<h2>/*F. Translate into the language. Four phase drill as usual.*/||</h2>

/*</i>The child is afraid.*/</i>||  tjitji nguḻu||
/*</i>The kangaroo is big.*/</i>||  maḻu puḻka||
/*</i>The man is unafraid.*/</i>||  wati rapa||
/*</i>The woman is tall.*/</i>||   minyma waṟa||
/*</i>Who is sick?*/</i>||   ngananya pikatjara||
/*</i>I am sick. (use single pronoun form)*/</i>||  ngayulu pikatjara||
/*</i>I am sick. (use short form)*/</i>||  pikatjara|ṉa#ngayulu#||
/*</i>I am sick. (emphatic form)*/</i>||  ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu# pikatjara||
/*</i>Who is happy?*/</i>||  ngananya pukuḻpa||
/*</i>This child is happy.*/</i>||  tjitji nyanga pukuḻpa||
/*</i>We all are tired. (short form)*/</i>||  paku|la#nganaṉa#||
/*</i>This kangaroo is big.*/</i>||  maḻu nyanga puḻka||
/*</i>They two are happy.*/</i>||  pula pukuḻpa||
/*</i>They all are happy.  (emphatic form)*/</i>||  tjana|ya#tjana# palya||
/*</i>They all are well. (short form)*/</i>||   palya|ya#tjana#||
/*</i>That far child is short.*/</i>||  tjitji nyara muṯumuṯu||
/*</i>These dogs are afraid.*/</i>||  papa nyanganpa nguḻu||
/*</i>This person is sick.*/</i>||  aṉangu nyanga pikatjara||
/*</i>These persons are well.*/</i>||  aṉangu nyanganpa palya||
/*</i>I am tired. (use shortest possible form)*/</i>||  paku|ṉa#ngayulu#||

/*</i>End of Unit 7*/</i>||

<h2>/*F. Translation into the language.*/||</h2>
<i>/*(Unless told otherwise please use the single pronoun form when
"I", "you", etc. occurs in the English cue).*/</i>||  
<i>/*The man is speaking.*/</i>||  wati wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||  
<i>/*I am speaking.*/</i>||    ngayulu wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||  
<i>/*We all are speaking.*/</i>||  nganaṉa wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||  
<i>/*The woman is sitting.*/</i>||  minyma nyinanyi#nyinanyi#||  
<i>/*The kangaroo is sitting.*/</i>||  maḻu nyinanyi#nyinanyi#||  
<i>/*You are standing.*/</i>||  nyuntu ngaṟanyi#ngaṟanyi#||  
<i>/*The child is coming.*/</i>||  tjitji pitjanyi#pitjanyi#||  
<i>/*The child came.*/</i>||    tjitji pitjangu#pitjanyi#||  
<i>/*The dog came.*/</i>||    papa pitjangu#pitjanyi#||  
<i>/*The person spoke.*/</i>||  aṉangu wangkangu#wangkanyi#||  
<i>/*The man stood.*/</i>||    wati ngaṟangu#ngaṟanyi#||  
<i>/*She stood.*/</i>||    paluṟu ngaṟangu#ngaṟanyi#||  
<i>/*The person come.*/</i>||  aṉangu pitjangu#pitjanyi#||  
<i>/*He is coming.*/</i>||    paluṟu pitjanyi#pitjanyi#||  
<i>/*That far man coming.*/</i>||  wati nyara pitjanyi#pitjanyi#||  
<i>/*Who is coming?*/</i>||    ngananya pitjanyi#pitjanyi#?||  
<i>/*Ingkatji is coming.*/</i>||  Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# pitjanyi#pitjanyi#.||  
<i>/*This one is speaking.*/</i>||  nyangatja wangkanyi#wangkanyi#.||  
<i>/*End of Unit 8*/</i>||

||<page><h1>/*Unit 10*/||</h1> 
<i>/*This is a lesson of practice and consolidation. It does not 
follow the pattern of the previous lessons. First we hear the 
English version of a dialogue, which you then hear in 
Pitjantjatjara. Listen carefully.*/</i>||
<h2>/*1. Dialogue*/||</h2>  
<i>/*A. What is your name?*/</i>|| 
<i>/*B. My name is Ingkatji.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*A. Do you speak Pitjantjatjara?*/</i>|| 
<i>/*B. Yes, I speak Pitjantjatjara. What about you?*/</i>|| 
<i>/*A. Yes, I speak Pitjantjatjaraa little. Later on I'll speak a lot.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*B. Are you well?*/</i>|| 
<i>/*A. Yes, I am well. What about you?*/</i>|| 
<i>/*B. I'm sick and I'm tired.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*A. Oh, sorry.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*Now listen to the same dialogue in Pitjantjatjara. Do not repeat.*/</i>|| 
/*A.*/ nyuntu ini ngananya? || 
/*B.*/ ngayulu ini Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|| 
/*A.*/ nyuntu Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#?|| 
/*B.*/ uwa, Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara#|ṉa#ngayulu# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| palu nyuntu?|| 
/*A.*/ uwa, ngayulu tjukutjuku wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| ngula|ṉa#ngayulu# puḻka wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
/*B.*/ nyuntu palya?|| 
/*A.*/ uwa, ngayulu palya|| palu nyuntu?|| 
/*B.*/ ngayulu pikatjara,|| munu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku|| 
/*A.*/ munta || 
<i>/*Now repeat the utterances of this dialogue one by one. Be careful 
to imitate the pronunciation and intonation exactly as the reader 
does it. Please listen to the dialogue once again. Do not repeat.*/</i>||
/*A.*/ nyuntu ini ngananya? || 
/*B.*/ ngayulu ini Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|| 
/*A.*/ nyuntu Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#?|| 
/*B.*/ uwa, Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara#|ṉa#ngayulu# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| palu nyuntu?||

ngula|ṉa#ngayulu# wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| pitjaku#pitjanyi#|| 
ngula|ṉa#ngayulu# pitjaku#pitjanyi#|| nyinaku#nyinanyi#||

<i>/*Model 6.*/</i>||
<i>/*In this drill you will hear two sentences. Link them 
together like this: 
You'll hear:*/</i>|| ngayulu pikatjara|| <i>/*(I am sick) and also*/</i>|| 
ngayulu paku|| <i>/*(I am tired) 
You say:*/</i>|| ngayulu pikatjara munu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku||
<i>/*meaning I am sick and I am tired.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*"munu" is the equivalent of "and" in sentences of this 
type. Note that it takes the short form of the personal pronoun.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu pikatjara|| ngayulu paku|| 
ngayulu pikatjara munu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku|| 
ngayulu palya|| ngayulu pukuḻpa|| 
ngayulu palya munu|ṉa#ngayulu# pukuḻpa|| 
ngayulu waṟa|| ngayulu puḻka||
ngayulu waṟa munu|ṉa#ngayulu# puḻka|| 
ngayulu nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| ngayulu wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| 
ngayulu nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| munu|ṉa#ngayulu# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| 
ngayulu pitjaku#pitjanyi#|| ngayulu wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
ngayulu pitjaku#pitjanyi# munu|ṉa#ngayulu# wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 7.*/</i>||
ngayulu pikatjara munu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku.|| <i>/*This sentence, meaning 
I am sick and I am tired, is to be converted into the 
you form (nyuntu) like this:*/</i>|| nyuntu pikatjara munu|n#nyuntu# paku|| 
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu pikatjara munu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku|| nyuntu||

paluṟu pikatjara munu paku|| ngali|| 
ngali pikatjara munu|li#ngali# paku|| nganaṉa|| 
nganaṉa pikatjara munu|la#nganaṉa# paku|| tjana|| 
tjana pikatjara munu|ya#tjana# paku|| 
<i>/*Model 8.*/</i>||
ngayulu nyinanyi#nyinanyi# munu|ṉa#ngayulu# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| nyuntu|| 
nyuntu nyinanyi#nyinanyi# munu|n#nyuntu# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| paluṟu||

tjana nyinanyi#nyinanyi# munu|ya#tjana# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 9.*/</i>||

ngali pitjaku#pitjanyi# munu|li#ngali# nyinaku#nyinanyi#|| nganaṉa||

<i>/*Model 10.*/</i>||
wati nyanga pikatjara munu paku|| minyma pala|| 
minyma pala pikatjara munu paku|| wati nyanganpa|| 
wati nyanganpa pikatjara munu|ya#tjana# paku|| tjitji palanpa|| 
tjitji palanpa pikatjara munu|ya#tjana# paku|| maḻu|| 
maḻu pikatjara munu paku|| papa nyaranpa|| 
papa nyaranpa pikatjara munu|ya#tjana# paku|| ngayulu|| 
ngayulu pikatjara munu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku|| 
<h2>/*3. Translate into the language.*/||</h2>
<i>/*This child is sick.*/</i>|| tjitji nyanga pikatjara|| 
<i>/*My name is Ingkatji*/</i>|| ngayulu ini Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|| 
<i>/*Do you speak Pitjantjatjara?*/</i>|| nyuntu Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara# wangkanyi#wangkanyi#?|| 
<i>/*This dog is sick and tired*/</i>|| papa nyanga pikatjara munu paku|| 
<i>/*What is your name?*/</i>|| nyuntu ini ngananya?|| 
<i>/*What is her name?*/</i>|| paluṟu ini ngananya?|| 
<i>/*What is this child's name?*/</i>|| tjitji nyanga ini ngananya?|| 
<i>/*Use single pronoun form:*/</i>|| 
<i>/*Later on I'll speak a lot.*/</i>|| ngayulu ngula puḻka wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
<i>/*What about you?*/</i>|| palu nyuntu?|| 
<i>/*What about him?*/</i>|| palu paluṟu?||
<i>/*No, I am sick and I am tired.*/</i>|| wiya, ngayulu pikatjara munu|ṉa#ngayulu# paku|| 
<i>/*These men are well and happy.*/</i>|| wati nyanganpa palya munu|ya#tjana# pukuḻpa.|| 
<i>/*We all will come and talk.*/</i>|| nganaṉa pitjaku#pitjanyi# munu|la#nganaṉa# wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
<i>/*They are all short and small.*/</i>|| tjana munu|ya#tjana# tjukutjuku|| 
<i>/*Are you all tired? Yes!!*/</i>|| nyura paku? uwa!!||  
<i>/*End of Unit 10*/</i>||

<h2>/*D. Now repeat and listen to the English meanings of the previous sentences.*/||</h2> 
nyuntu wangka#wangkanyi#!|| <i>/*You talk!*/</i>|| 
nyupali wangka#wangkanyi#!|| <i>/*You two talk! (speak)*/</i>|| 
nyura wangka#wangkanyi#!|| <i>/*You all talk!*/</i>||

nyupali pitja#pitjanyi#!|| <i>/*You two come!*/</i>|| 
nyura pitja#pitjanyi#!|| <i>/*You all come!*/</i>||

nyupali wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!||  <i>/*You two run!*/</i>||

wangka#wangkanyi#!||  <i>/*You speak!*/</i>|| 
<i>/*The following are short forms of commands:*/</i>|| 
wangka#wangkanyi#|pula!|| <i>/*You two talk!*/</i>|| 
wangka#wangkanyi#|ya#tjana#!|| <i>/*You all speak!*/</i>|| 
pitja#pitjanyi#!|| <i>/*You come!*/</i>|| 
pitja#pitjanyi#|pula!|| <i>/*You two come!*/</i>|| 
pitja#pitjanyi#|ya#tjana#!|| <i>/*You all come!*/</i>|| 
wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!|| <i>/*You run!*/</i>||

wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#|ya#tjana#!|| <i>/*You all run!*/</i>||
<i>/*Now reverting to ordinary sentences:*/</i>||
maḻu wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#|| <i>/*The kangaroo is running.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#|| <i>/*I am running.*/</i>|| 
paluṟu wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#|| <i>/*He is running. (also she/it)*/</i>|| 
wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#|ya#tjana#|| <i>/*They are running. ( short form)*/</i>|| 
maḻu wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#|| <i>/*The kangaroo ran.*/</i>|| 
maḻu wirtjapakalku#wirtjapakaṉi#|| <i>/*The kangaroo will run*/</i>|| 
tjitji punkaṉi#punkaṉi#|| <i>/*The child is falling.*/</i>|| 
tjitji punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|| <i>/*The child fell.*/</i>||
tjitji nyara punkalku#punkaṉi#|| <i>/*That far child will fall*/</i>|| 
punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|li#ngali#|| <i>/*We two fell. (short form)*/</i>|| 
tjitji wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# munu punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|| <i>/*The child ran and fell.*/</i>|| 
tjitji punkaṉu#punkaṉi# munu ulangu#ulanyi#|| <i>/*The child fell and cried.*/</i>||

<h2>/*E. Drills*/||</h2>
<i>/*In the first drill please convert from the present 
tense to the imperative or command form. Like this:*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You will hear:*/</i>|| nyuntu wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| <i>/*(you are talking)*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| nyuntu wangka#wangkanyi#|| <i>/*(you talk)*/</i>||
<i>/*Off you go. 
Model 1.*/</i>||
nyuntu wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||   nyuntu wangka#wangkanyi#!|| 
nyuntu pitjanyi#pitjanyi#||    nyuntu pitja#pitjanyi#!|| 
nyuntu wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#||   nyuntu wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!|| 
nyuntu punkaṉi#punkaṉi#||   nyuntu punkala#punkaṉi#!|| 
nyuntu nyinanyi#nyinanyi#||   nyuntu nyina!|| 
<i>/*Model 2.*/</i>||
nyupali wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||   nyupali wangka#wangkanyi#!|| 
nyupali pitjanyi#pitjanyi#||   nyupali pitja#pitjanyi#!|| 
nyura wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||   nyura wangka#wangkanyi#!||
nyupali wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#||   nyupali wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!|| 
nyura punkaṉi#punkaṉi#||   nyura punkala#punkaṉi#!|| 
<i>/*Model 3.*/</i>||
<i>/*Convert from the long fom of the command to the short form, like this:*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| nyuntu wangka#wangkanyi#|| 
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| wangka#wangkanyi#!||
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>|| 
nyuntu wangka#wangkanyi#!||  wangka#wangkanyi#!|| 
nyuntu pitja#pitjanyi#!||  pitja#pitjanyi#!||
nyuntu wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!||   wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!|| 
nyupali wangka#wangkanyi#||  wangka#wangkanyi#|pula!|| 
nyupali wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!||   wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#|pula!|| 
nyura pitja#pitjanyi#||   pitja#pitjanyi#|ya#tjana#!|| 
nyura wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!||   wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#|ya#tjana#!||
nyura nyina!||   nyina|ya#tjana#!||
<i>/*Model 4.*/</i>||
<i>/*Tenses. Hear a statement and a cue.
Use the cue to form your new sentence.
Off you go.*/</i>|| 
wati wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||   wangkangu#wangkanyi#|| 
wati wangkangu#wangkanyi#||   minyma|| 
minyma wangkangu#wangkanyi#||   tjitji pala|| 
tjitji pala wangkangu#wangkanyi#||   wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
tjitji pala wangkaku#wangkanyi#||   pitjaku#pitjanyi#|| 
tjitji pala pitjaku#pitjanyi#||   pitjangu#pitjanyi#|| 
tjitji pala pitjangu#pitjanyi#||  maḻu|| 
maḻu pitjangu#pitjanyi#||   nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| 
maḻu nyinanyi#nyinanyi#||   wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#|| 
maḻu wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#||   wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#|| 
maḻu wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#||   tjitji|| 
tjitji wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#||   punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|| 
tjitji punkaṉu#punkaṉi#||   punkalku#punkaṉi#|| 
tjitji punkalku#punkaṉi#||   wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
tjitji wangkaku#wangkanyi#||   ulaku#ulanyi#|| 
tjitji ulaku#ulanyi#||   minyma|| 
minyma ulaku#ulanyi#||   pitjaku#pitjanyi#|| 
minyma pitjaku#pitjanyi#||   pitjanyi#pitjanyi#|| 
minyma pitjanyi#pitjanyi#||   wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| 
minyma wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||   wati|| 
wati wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 5*/</i>||.
<i>/*Conversion from present to past tense. Off you go.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu pitjanyi#pitjanyi#||   ngayulu pitjangu#pitjanyi#|| 
pitjanyi#pitjanyi#|ṉa#ngayulu#||   pitjangu#pitjanyi#|ṉa#ngayulu#||

wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#|ṉa#ngayulu#||    wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#|ṉa#ngayulu#||
ngayulu punkaṉi#punkaṉi#||   ngayulu punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|| 
punkaṉi#punkaṉi#|ṉa#ngayulu#||   punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|ṉa#ngayulu#|| 
<i>/*Now a few with nyuntu and paluṟu*/</i>||

<i>/*The man is running.*/</i>|| wati wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#||

<i>/*You two come!*/</i>|| nyupali pitja#pitjanyi#!|| 
<i>/*You all run!*/</i>||   nyura wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!|| 
<i>/*You come! (short form)*/</i>||  pitja#pitjanyi#!|| 
<i>/*You two speak! (short form)*/</i>||  wangka#wangkanyi#|pula!|| 
<i>/*You all run! (short form)*/</i>||   wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#|ya#tjana#!|| 
<i>/*He is running. (short form)*/</i>||   wirtjapakaṉi#wirtjapakaṉi#|| 
<i>/*The child ran and fell.*/</i>||   tjitji wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# munu punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|| 
<i>/*I will run.*/</i>|| ngayulu wirtjapakalku#wirtjapakaṉi#|| 
<i>/*I will run. ( short form)*/</i>||   wirtjapakalku#wirtjapakaṉi#|ṉa#ngayulu#|| 
<i>/*We all will speak.*/</i>|| nganaṉa wangkaku#wangkanyi#|| 
<i>/*We all will speak. ( short form)*/</i>||  wangkaku#wangkanyi#|la#nganaṉa#|| 
<i>/*You all come!*/</i>|| nyura pitja#pitjanyi#!|| 
<i>/*You all come! (short form)*/</i>||   pitja#pitjanyi#|ya#tjana#!|| 
<i>/*You two run!*/</i>|| nyupali wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#!|| 
<i>/*You two run! ( short form)*/</i>|| wirtjapakala#wirtjapakaṉi#|pula!||

ngali maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
maḻu|li#ngali# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
nganaṉa maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
maḻu|la#nganaṉa# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
tjana maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
maḻu|ya#tjana# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
nyupali maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
nyura maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
pula maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
<h2>/*D. Now listen once again and fix the English meanings in your mind.*/||</h2> 
wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉi#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*The man is spearing a kangaroo.*/</i>||
wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*The man sees a kangaroo.*/</i>||
aṉangu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉi#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*The person is spearing the kangaroo.*/</i>||
aṉangu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*The person sees the kangaroo.*/</i>||
wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*The man speared a kangaroo.*/</i>||
wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#||  <i>/*The man saw a kangaroo.*/</i>||
tjitji|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*The child saw a kangaroo.*/</i>||
minyma|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*The woman saw a kangaroo.*/</i>||
Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*Ingkatji speared a kangaroo.*/</i>||
Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu# kaḻaya nyangu#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*Ingkatji saw an emu*/</i>||
Waṯulya#Waṯulya#|lu#-lu# kaḻaya nyangu#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*Watulya saw an emu.*/</i>||
Waṯulya#Waṯulya#|lu#-lu# kanyaḻa nyangu#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*Watulya saw a euro.*/</i>||
ngayulu kaḻaya wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*I speared an emu.*/</i>||
ngayulu maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*I saw a kangaroo.*/</i>||
kaḻaya|ṉa#ngayulu# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*I speared an emus (short form)*/</i>||
maḻu|ṉa#ngayulu# nyangu#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*I saw a kangaroo. (short form)*/</i>||
nyuntu maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*You speared a kangaroo*/</i>||
maḻu|n#nyuntu# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*You speared a kangaroo. (short form)*/</i>||
paluṟu maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*He speared a kangaroo.*/</i>||
maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*He speared a kangaroo. (short form)*/</i>||
ngali maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*We two speared a kangaroo.*/</i>||
maḻu|li#ngali# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*We two speared a 'roo. (short form)*/</i>||
nganaṉa maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*We all speared a kangaroo.*/</i>||
maḻu|la#nganaṉa# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*We all speared a roo.(short form)*/</i>||
tjana maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*They all speared a 'roo.*/</i>||
maḻu|ya#tjana# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*They all speared a 'roo. (short form)*/</i>||
nyupali maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*You two speared a 'roo. (No short form)*/</i>||
nyura maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*You all speared a 'roo. (No short form)*/</i>||
pula maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*They two speared a 'roo. (No short form)*/</i>||
<h2>/*E. Drills.*/||</h2>
<i>/*Model 1.*/</i>||
<i>/*Substitution of subjects in transitive sentences.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You'll hear:*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*(the man sees the 'roo)*/</i>|| tjitji|| 
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| tjitji|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||  <i>/*(the child sees the kangaroo)*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You are to substitute the new cue only in the subject 
slot. You will note in transitive sentences the 
subject has a special suffix. This suffix is "ngku" 
on common nouns ending in a vowel; it is "lu" on 
proper nouns. Off you go.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*Model 1.*/</i>||
wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||    tjitji|| 
tjitji|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   minyma|| 
minyma|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   aṉangu|| 
aṉangu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa|| 
papa|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||
<i>/*Now the model is changed. Listen again.*/</i>||
wati|ngku#-ngku# minyma nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   tjitji|| 
tjitji|ngku#-ngku# minyma nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   maḻu|| 
maḻu|ngku#-ngku# minyma nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa|| 
papa|ngku#-ngku# minyma nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   kaḻaya|| 
kaḻaya#kaḻaya#|ngku#-ngku# minyma nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   kanyaḻa|| 
kanyaḻa#kanyaḻa#|ngku#-ngku# minyma nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 2.*/</i>||
<i>/*Now with proper nouns. Remember -the ending is "lu". 
Off you go.*/</i>|| 
Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Tinimayi#Tinimayi#|| 
Tinimayi#Tinimayi#|lu#-lu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Waṯulya#Waṯulya#|lu#-lu#|| 
Waṯulya#Waṯulya#|lu#-lu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Wangilyi#Wangilyi#|| 
Wangilyi#Wangilyi#|lu#-lu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 3.*/</i>||
<i>/*Now with common nouns as subject and proper nouns as 
object. The subject will be the cue.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   tjitji|| 
tjitji|ngku#-ngku# Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   minyma|| 
minyma|ngku#-ngku# Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   maḻu|| 
maḻu|ngku#-ngku# Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 4.*/</i>||
<i>/*Now with a pronoun as subject (nonsuffix) and a 
common noun as object.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| ngayulu maḻu wakalku#wakaṉi#|| <i>/*(I will spear a 'roo)*/</i>||   nyuntu||  
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| nyuntu maḻu wakalku#wakaṉi#|| <i>/*(You will spear a 'roo).*/</i>||
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu maḻu wakalku#wakaṉi#||   nyuntu||
nyuntu maḻu wakalku#wakaṉi#||   paluṟu|| 
paluṟu maḻu wakalku#wakaṉi#||   ngali|| 
ngali maḻu wakalku#wakaṉi#||   tjana|| 
tjana maḻu wakalku#wakaṉi#|| 
<i>/*New model with the verb nyanganyi.*/</i>||
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   nyuntu|| 
nyuntu papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   paluṟu|| 
paluṟu papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   nganaṉa|| 
nganaṉa papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   nyura|| 
nyura papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 5.*/</i>||
<i>/*Now we shall present a sentence in which the subject 
continues to be a personal pronoun and the object 
will be a proper noun. Substitution in the subject 
slot. Off you go.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   paluṟu||
paluṟu Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   ngali|| 
ngali Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   nyuntu|| 
nyuntu Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   tjana|| 
tjana Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Model 6.*/</i>||
<i>/*You are now asked to convert from the single pronoun 
form to the short form. Like this:*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You will hear:*/</i>|| ngayulu maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*(I see a 'roo)*/</i>|| 
<i>/*You will say:*/</i>|| maḻu|ṉa#ngayulu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*(I see a 'roo) short form.*/</i>||
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   maḻu|ṉa#ngayulu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
nyuntu maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   maḻu|n#nyuntu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
paluṟu maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
ngali maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   maḻu|li#ngali# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
tjana maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   maḻu|ya#tjana# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Now with "papa" instead of "maḻu".*/</i>|| 
ngayulu papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa|ṉa#ngayulu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
nyuntu papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa|n#nyuntu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
paluṟu papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
nganaṉa papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa|la#nganaṉa# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
ngali papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa|li#ngali# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
tjana papa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   papa|ya#tjana# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Now with a proper noun as object.*/</i>|| 
ngayulu Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||  Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|ṉa#ngayulu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
nyuntu Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|n#nyuntu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
paluṟu Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
ngali Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|li#ngali# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
nganaṉa Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|la#nganaṉa# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
tjana Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||   Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#|ya#tjana# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<h2>/*F. Translation into the language.*/||</h2> 
<i>/*The man sees a 'roo.</i>*/||   wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*The child sees a 'roo.</i>*/||   tjitji|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*I see a 'roo.</i>*/||   ngayulu maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*We all see a 'roo.</i>*/||   nganaṉa maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Ingkatji sees an emu.</i>*/|| Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu# kaḻaya nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Watulya sees an emu.</i>*/|| Waṯulya#Waṯulya#|lu#-lu# kaḻaya nyangu#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*The man saw an emu.</i>*/||   wati|ngku#-ngku# kaḻaya nyangu#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*The man speared a 'roo.</i>*/||   wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| 
<i>/*I saw an emu.</i>*/||  ngayulu kaḻaya nyangu#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*I saw an emu and speared it.</i>*/||  ngayulu kaḻaya nyangu#nyanganyi# munu|ṉa#ngayulu# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| 
<i>/*In the following five translations use short forms only:</i>*/|| 
<i>/*I see a woman.</i>*/||   minyma|ṉa#ngayulu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*We two saw a woman.</i>*/||   minyma|li#ngali# nyangu#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*We all will spear an emu.</i>*/||   kaḻaya|la#nganaṉa# wakalku#wakaṉi#|| 
<i>/*They all saw the child.</i>*/||   tjitji|ya#tjana# nyangu#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*Did you spear a 'roo?</i>*/||   maḻu|n#nyuntu# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#?|| 
<i>/*You spear the roo!</i>*/||   nyuntu maḻu wakala#wakaṉi#!|| 
<i>/*You spear the emu!</i>*/||   nyuntu kaḻaya wakala#wakaṉi#!|| 
<i>/*You look at that far woman.</i>*/||   nyuntu minyma nyara nyawa#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*You look at the big man.</i>*/||   nyuntu wati puḻka nyawa#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*You speak Pitjantjatjara!</i>*/||   nyuntu Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara# wangka#wangkanyi#!|| 
<i>/*End of Unit 12</i>*/||

<h2>/*B. Listen and repeat the following and fix the English meanings in your mind.*/||</h2>

<h2>/*D. Repeat these sentences again and fix the English in your mind.*/||</h2> 
wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayunya#ngayulu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees me.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# nyuntunya#nyuntu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees you.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# palunya#paluṟu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees him/her/it.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# ngalinya#ngali# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees us two.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# nyupalinya#nyupali# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees you two.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# pulanya#pula# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees them two.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# nganaṉanya#nganaṉa# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees us all.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# nyuranya#nyura# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees you all.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# tjananya#tjana# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees them all.*/</i>|| 
<i>/*Short forms:*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku#|ṉi#ngayulu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*The man sees me.*/</i>||

uwa#unganyi#|ṉi#ngayulu#|| <i>/*Give it to me (short form)*/</i>||

<i>/*The woman will go to Ernabella.*/</i>|| minyma Aṉapala#Aṉapala#|la#-la#|kutu#-kutu# ankuku#ananyi#|| 
<i>/*Where is the man coming from?*/</i>|| wati yaaltji|nguṟu#-nguṟu# pitjanyi#pitjanyi#?|| 
<i>/*Where the woman come from?*/</i>|| minyma yaaltji|nguṟu#-nguṟu# pitjaku#pitjanyi#?|| 
<i>/*Where did the roo come from?*/</i>|| maḻu yaaltji|nguṟu#-nguṟu# pitjangu#pitjanyi#?||

<i>/*Where are you going?*/</i>|| yaaltji|kutu#-kutu#|n#nyuntu# ananyi#ananyi#||

ngunytju|| <i>/*mother*/</i>||

kamuṟu|| <i>/*uncle (mother's brother)*/</i>||

kuḻaṯa|| <i>/*spear*/</i>|| 
piti|| <i>/*carrying dish (coolimon)*/</i>|| 
wana|| <i>/*digging stick*/</i>||

palyaṉu#palyaṉi#|| <i>/*made*/</i>||

rungkala#rungkaṉi#!|| <i>/*hit! (with boomerang)*/</i>||

wati|ku#-ku# katja pikatjara|| <i>/*The man's son is sick.*/</i>|| 
tjitji|ku#-ku# mama pitjanyi#pitjanyi#|| <i>/*The child's father is coming.*/</i>||

nganampa#nganaṉa# mama pukuḻpa|| <i>/*Our father is happy.*/</i>|| 
wati|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| <i>/*The man is making a boomerang.*/</i>|| 
nyuntu kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#?|| <i>/*Are you making a boomerang?*/</i>|| 
wiya, ngayulu kuḻaṯa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| <i>/*No, I'm making a spear.*/</i>||
ngayulu kuḻaṯa palyaṉu#palyaṉi#|| <i>/*I made a spear.*/</i>|| 
paluṟu kaḻi palyalku#palyaṉi#|| <i>/*He will make a boomerang.*/</i>|| 
nyuntu kanyaḻa rungkala#rungkaṉi#!|| <i>/*You hit the euro!*/</i>||

wati|ngku#-ngku# minyma|ku#-ku# piti palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| <i>/*The man is making a carrying dish for the woman.*/</i>||

ngayulu nyuntumpa#nyuntu# kuḻaṯa palyalku#palyaṉi#|| <i>/*I shall make a spear for you.*/</i>||

<i>/*Model 2*/</i>||
<i>/*Four phase drill as usual:*/</i>||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| wati nyanga|ngku#-ngku#||

wati muṯumuṯu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| wati nyanga puḻka|ngku#-ngku#||
