wati nyara puḻka|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
<i>/*Model 3*/</i>||
<i>/*Four Phase drill.*/</i>||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| nyuntumpa#nyuntu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku#||	
nyuntumpa#nyuntu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| palumpa#paluṟu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku#||	
palumpa#paluṟu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| palumpa#paluṟu# mama|ngku#-ngku#||	
palumpa#paluṟu# mama|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ngalimpa mama|ngku#-ngku#||	
ngalimpa mama|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| tjanampa#tjana# mama|ngku#-ngku#||	
tjanampa#tjana# mama|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| nyurampa#nyura# mama|ngku#-ngku#||	
nyurampa#nyura# mama|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| nyurampa#nyura# katja|ngku#-ngku#||	
nyurampa#nyura# katja|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ngayuku#ngayulu# katja|ngku#-ngku#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# katja|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| nyuntumpa#nyuntu# katja|ngku#-ngku#||	
nyuntumpa#nyuntu# katja|ngku#-ngku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#||	
<i>/*Model 4*/</i>||
<i>/*Four phase drill. You will hear a sentence like:*/</i>||	
wati ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| <i>/*The man is sitting in camp.*/</i>||	
<i>/*You are asked to replace*/</i>|| "ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#"|| <i>/*with*/</i>||	
maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| <i>/*and make the appropriate change in	
the subject, like this:*/</i>||	
"wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#."||
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||	
wati ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
minyma ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| minyma|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
tjitji ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| tjitji|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
aṉangu ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| aṉangu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||
papa ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| papa|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
wati nyanga ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| wati nyanga|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
<i>/*Now we give you a few examples of similar sentences in which	
the subject phrase ends in a consonant. Just listen and	
repeat.*/</i>||	
Wintjin#Wintjin#|nga#-nga# ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#||	
Wintjin#Wintjin#|tu#-tu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# uṉṯalpa ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# uṉṯal#uṉṯalpa#|tu#-tu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻanypa ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻany#maḻanypa#|tju#-tju# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
tjitji nyanganpa ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| 
tjitji nyangan#nyanganpa#|tu#-tu# maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| 
<h2>/*F. Translate into the language.*/||</h2>
<i>/*My wife is happy.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# kuri pukuḻpa|| 
<i>/*My father saw a roo.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# mama|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*My older brother saw an emu.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# kaḻaya nyangu#nyanganyi#|| 
<i>/*My mother will sit in camp.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# ngunytju ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinaku#nyinanyi#|| 
<i>/*My uncle hit an emu with a boomerang.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# kamuṟu|ngku#-ngku# kaḻaya kaḻi|ngka#-ngka# rungkaṉu#rungkaṉi#|| 
<i>/*My father is tall.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# mama waṟa|| 
<i>/*Is your mother sick?*/</i>|| nyuntumpa#nyuntu# ngunytju pikatjara?|| 
<i>/*Their dog is small.*/</i>|| tjanampa#tjana# papa tjukutjuku|| 
<i>/*The man made a boomerang for me.*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayuku#ngayulu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#|| 
<i>/*I made a boomerang for this child*/</i>|| ngayulu tjitji nyanga|ku#-ku# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#|| 
<i>/*The child's father is coming.*/</i>|| tjitji|ku#-ku# mama pitjanyi#pitjanyi#|| 
<i>/*My older brother is sick.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa pikatjara|| 
<i>/*You hit the euro with a boomerang!*/</i>|| nyuntu kanyaḻa kaḻi|ngka#-ngka# rungkala#rungkaṉi#!|| 
<i>/*The man speared a roo with a spear.*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu kuḻaṯa|ngka#-ngka# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
<i>/*(Short form)*/</i>|| 
<i>/*I speared it with a spear.*/</i>|| kuḻaṯa|ngka#-ngka#|ṉa#ngayulu# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| 
<i>/*(Short form)*/</i>|| 
<i>/*The man made a boomerang for me.*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku#|tju#ngayulu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#|| 
<i>/*The man will make a carrying dish for the woman.*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# minyma|ku#-ku# piti palyalku#palyaṉi#|| 
<i>/*(Short form)*/</i>|| 
<i>/*The man will make a carrying dish for her.*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku#|ra#-ra# piti palyalku#palyaṉi#|| 
<i>/*End of Unit 15*/</i>||


||<page><h1>/*Unit 16*/||</h1>
<h2>/*1. Dialogue*/||</h2> 
<i>/*You will now hear the English version of a dialogue, which you will	
later hear in Pitjantjatjara.*/</i>||	
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| <i>/*What are you two making?*/</i>||	
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| <i>/*I am making a boomerang and my older brother is making a spear.*/</i>|| <i>/*And where are you two going?*/</i>||	
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| <i>/*I am going to the mountain for meat, and my wife is going to the creek for vegetable food.*/</i>||	
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| <i>/*When will you two come back?*/</i>||	
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| <i>/*We'll come back today.*/</i>||	
<i>/*Now listen to the same dialogue in Pitjantjatjara. Do not repeat.*/</i>||	
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| nyupali nyaa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#?||	
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| ngayulu kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# kuḻaṯa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#||	
palu nyupali yaaltji|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi#?||	
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| ngayulu apu|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi# kuka|ku#-ku#|| ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuri karu|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi# mai|ku#-ku#.||
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| nyupali yaalaṟa ngalya pitjaku#pitjanyi#?||
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| kuwari|li#ngali# pitjanyi#pitjanyi#.||	
<i>/*Now repeat the utterances of the dialogue one by one. Be careful	
to imitate the pronuciation and the intonation exactly as the	
speaker does it.*/</i>||
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| nyupali nyaa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#?||	
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| ngayulu kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# kuḻaṯa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#||	
palu nyupali yaaltji|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi#?||	
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| ngayulu apu|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi# kuka|ku#-ku#|| ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuri karu|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi# mai|ku#-ku#.||
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| nyupali yaalaṟa ngalya pitjaku#pitjanyi#?||
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| kuwari|li#ngali# pitjanyi#pitjanyi#.||
<i>/*Please listen to the dialogue once again. Do not repeat.*/</i>||
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| nyupali nyaa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#?||	
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| ngayulu kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# kuḻaṯa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#||	
palu nyupali yaaltji|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi#?||	
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| ngayulu apu|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi# kuka|ku#-ku#|| ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuri karu|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi# mai|ku#-ku#.||
<i>/*B.*/</i>|| nyupali yaalaṟa ngalya pitjaku#pitjanyi#?||
<i>/*A.*/</i>|| kuwari|li#ngali# pitjanyi#pitjanyi#.||
<h2>/*2. Structural Drills*/||</h2> 	
<i>/*Model 1.*/</i>||
<i>/*Conjoined sentences. You will hear two sentences.	
You are asked to join them, like this:*/</i>||	
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| <i>/*and also*/</i>|| wati wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||	
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi# munta wangkanyi#wangkanyi#.|| <i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||	
wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| wati wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||	
wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi# munu wangkanyi#wangkanyi#||	
tjitji pitjanyi#pitjanyi#|| tjitji ulanyi#ulanyi#||	
tjitji pitjanyi#pitjanyi# munu ulanyi#ulanyi#.||	
tjitji wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#|| tjitji punkaṉu#punkaṉi#||	
tjitji wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# munu punkaṉu#punkaṉi#.||	
ngayulu kuḻaṯa palyaṉu#palyaṉi#|| ngayulu maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
ngayulu kuḻaṯa palyaṉu#palyaṉi# munu|ṉa#ngayulu# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
wati Aṉapala#Aṉapala#|la#-la#|kutu#-kutu# anu#ananyi#|| wati|ngku#-ngku# Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyangu#nyanganyi#||	
wati Aṉapala#Aṉapala#|la#-la#|kutu#-kutu# anu#ananyi# munu Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyangu#nyanganyi#||
ngali Aṉapala#Aṉapala#|la#-la#|kutu#-kutu# anu#ananyi#|| ngali Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara# wangkangu#wangkanyi#||	
ngali Aṉapala#Aṉapala#|la#-la#|kutu#-kutu# anu#ananyi# munu|li#ngali# Pitjantjatjara#Pitjantjatjara# wangkangu#wangkanyi#.||	
<i>/*Model 2*/</i>||
<i>/*In the last drill you were asked to join sentences	
having the same subject. In this drill you will hear	
two sentences with different subjects. Join them	
together, like this:*/</i>||	
<i>/*You'll hear:*/</i>|| wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| <i>/*and also:*/</i>|| minyma ngaṟanyi#ngaṟanyi#||	
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi# ka minyma ngaṟanyi#ngaṟanyi#.||	
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||	
wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi#|| minyma ngaṟanyi#ngaṟanyi#||	
wati nyinanyi#nyinanyi# ka minyma ngaṟanyi#ngaṟanyi#.||	
minyma wangkanyi#wangkanyi#|| tjitji ulanyi#ulanyi#||	
minyma wangkanyi#wangkanyi# ka tjitji ulanyi#ulanyi#||	
wati kuka|ku#-ku# anu#ananyi#|| minyma mai|ku#-ku# anu#ananyi#||	
wati kuka|ku#-ku# anu#ananyi# ka minyma mai|ku#-ku# anu#ananyi#.||	
ngayulu maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻany#maḻanypa#|tju#-tju# kanyaḻa	wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
ngayulu maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi# ka ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻany#maḻanypa#|tju#-tju# kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#.||	
ngayulu ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinaku#nyinanyi#|| ngayuku#ngayulu# kuri mai|ku#-ku# ankuku#ananyi#||
ngayulu ngura|ngka#-ngka# nyinaku#nyinanyi# ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuri mai|ku#-ku# ankuku#ananyi#||	
<i>/*Model 3*/</i>||
<i>/*In the following you will hear two sentences	
having different subjects. The object of the	
first sentence will be the same as the subject	
of the second. Join them using short forms of	
the pronouns, like this:*/</i>||	
<i>/*You'll hear:*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayunya#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi#|| <i>/*(the man hit me)*/</i>|| <i>/*and also*/</i>|| ngayulu punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|| <i>/*(I fell over)*/</i>||
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayunya#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi# ka|ṉa#ngayulu# punkaṉu#punkaṉi#|| <i>/*(the man hit me and I fell over)*/</i>||	
<i>/*Off you go:*/</i>||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayunya#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi#|| ngayulu punkaṉu#punkaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayunya#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi# ka|ṉa#ngayulu# punkaṉu#punkaṉi#||
wati|ngku#-ngku# nyuntunya#nyuntu# pungu#punganyi#|| nyuntu ulangu#ulanyi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# nyuntunya#nyuntu# pungu#punganyi# ka|n#nyuntu# ulangu#ulanyi#.||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# tjitji pungu#punganyi#|| tjitji ulangu#ulanyi#||
wati|ngku#-ngku# tjitji pungu#punganyi# ka ulangu#ulanyi#.||	
ngayulu maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#|| maḻu wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#||
ngayulu maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi# ka wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#.||	
tjana ngalinya#ngali# pungu#punganyi#|| ngali punkaṉu#punkaṉi#||	
tjana ngalinya#ngali# pungu#punganyi# ka|li#ngali# punkaṉu#punkaṉi#.||	
tjana nganaṉanya#nganaṉa# pungu#punganyi#|| nganaṉa punkaṉu#punkaṉi#||	
tjana nganaṉanya#nganaṉa# pungu#punganyi# ka|la#nganaṉa# punkaṉu#punkaṉi#.||	
<i>/*Model 4.*/</i>||
<i>/*You will hear a question, give an appropriate answer	
using the short forms of the pronouns. Like this:*/</i>||	
<i>/*You hear:*/</i>|| nyuntu yaalaṟa pitjangu#pitjanyi#?||	
<i>/*(When did you come?)*/</i>||	
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| kuwari|ṉa#ngayulu# pitjangu#pitjanyi#.|| <i>/*(I came today.)*/</i>||	
<i>/*Off you go:*/</i>||	
nyuntu yaalaṟa pitjangu#pitjanyi#?||	
kuwari|ṉa#ngayulu# pitjangu#pitjanyi#||	
nyupali yaalaṟa pitjangu#pitjanyi#?||	
kuwari|li#ngali# pitjangu#pitjanyi#.||	
nyura yaalaṟa pitjangu#pitjanyi#?||	
kuwari|la#nganaṉa# pitjangu#pitjanyi#.||	
tjana yaalaṟa pitjangu#pitjanyi#?||	
kuwari|ya#tjana# pitjangu#pitjanyi#.||	
paluṟu yaalaṟa pitjangu#pitjanyi#?||	
kuwari pitjangu#pitjanyi#.||	
<i>/*Model 5.*/</i>||
<i>/*Random substitutions. You will hear a sentence and a	
cue. Use the cue to form a new sentence. Four phase	
drill as usual. Off you go.*/</i>||	
ngayulu kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| kuḻaṯa||	
ngayulu kuḻaṯa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| piti||	
ngayulu piti palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| wati|ngku#-ngku#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# piti palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻany#maḻanypa#|tju#-tju#||	
ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻany#maḻanypa#|tju#-tju# piti palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| nyuntumpa#nyuntu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku#||	
nyuntumpa#nyuntu# kuṯa|ngku#-ngku# piti palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| nganampa#nganaṉa# mama|ngku#-ngku#||	
nganampa#nganaṉa# mama|ngku#-ngku# piti palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| wiltja||	
nganampa#nganaṉa# mama|ngku#-ngku# wiltja palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| ngayulu||	
ngayulu wiltja palyaṉi#palyaṉi#|| nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
ngayulu wiltja nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| maḻu||	
ngayulu maḻu nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| kanyaḻa||	
ngayulu kanyaḻa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| wati|ngku#-ngku#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# kanyaḻa nyanganyi#nyanganyi#|| nyangu#nyanganyi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# kanyaḻa nyangu#nyanganyi#|| wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| aṉangu|ngku#-ngku#||	
aṉangu|ngku#-ngku# kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| paluṟu||	
paluṟu kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| tjana||	
tjana kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| pula||	
pula kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#|| nyangu#nyanganyi#||	
pula kanyaḻa nyangu#nyanganyi#|| wati|ngku#-ngku#||
wati|ngku#-ngku# kanyaḻa nyangu#nyanganyi#|| Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu#||	
Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu# kanyaḻa nyangu#nyanganyi#|| Wintjin#Wintjin#|nga#-nga#||	
Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|lu#-lu# Wintjin#Wintjin#|nga#-nga# nyangu#nyanganyi#|| tjitji|ngku#-ngku#||	
tjitji|ngku#-ngku# Wintjin#Wintjin#|nga#-nga# nyangu#nyanganyi#|| Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya#||	
tjitji|ngku#-ngku# Ingkatji#Ingkatji#|nya#-nya# nyangu#nyanganyi#||
<i>/*Model 6.*/</i>||
<i>/*Review of short forms — subject. You will hear a	
sentence using the single pronoun subject form.	
Convert this to the short form, like this:*/</i>||	
<i>/*You will hear:*/</i>|| ngayulu maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#||	
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| maḻu|ṉa#ngayulu# nyangu#nyanganyi#||
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||	
ngayulu maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#||	
maḻu|ṉa#ngayulu# nyangu#nyanganyi#.||
nyuntu kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||
kaḻi|n#nyuntu# palyaṉu#palyaṉi#.||	
paluṟu kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
kanyaḻa wakaṉu#wakaṉi#.||	
ngali kuka|ku#-ku# ananyi#ananyi#||	
kuka|ku#-ku#|li#ngali# ananyi#ananyi#||	
nganaṉa kuka|ku#-ku# ananyi#ananyi#||
kuka|ku#-ku#|la#nganaṉa# ananyi#ananyi#.||	
tjana ngura|kutu#-kutu# ananyi#ananyi#||	
ngura|kutu#-kutu#|ya#tjana# ananyi#ananyi#.||
<i>/*Model 7.*/</i>||
<i>/*Review of short forms - object. You will hear a	
sentence using the single pronoun object form.	
Convert this to the short form. Like this:*/</i>||	
<i>/*You will hear:*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayunya#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi#||	
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku#|ṉi#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi#||	
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayunya#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku#|ṉi#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# nyuntunya#nyuntu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||
wati|ngku#-ngku#|nta#nyuntu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# palunya#paluṟu# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
minyma|ngku#-ngku# ngalinya#ngali# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||
minyma|ngku#-ngku#|linya#ngali# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
minyma|ngku#-ngku# nganaṉanya#nganaṉa# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
minyma|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||
<i>/*Model 8.*/</i>||
<i>/*Review of short forms — dative. You will hear a	
sentence using the single pronoun dative form.	
Convert to the short form like this:*/</i>||	
<i>/*You will hear:*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayuku#ngayulu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
<i>/*You say:*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku#|tju#ngayulu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# ngayuku#ngayulu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku#|tju#ngayulu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# nyuntumpa#nyuntu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku#|nku#-nku# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# palumpa#paluṟu# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku#|ra#-ra# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# ngalimpa kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku#|limpa#ngali# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku# nganampa#nganaṉa# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
wati|ngku#-ngku#|lampa#nganaṉa# kaḻi palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||

<h2>/*3. Translate into the language.*/||</h2> 	
<i>/*The man is making a boomerang for the child.*/</i>|| wati|ngku#-ngku# tjitji|ku#-ku# kaḻi palyaṉi#palyaṉi#||
<i>/*Wintjin is making a spear for my younger brother.*/</i>|| Wintjin#Wintjin#|tu#-tu# ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻany#maḻanypa#|ku#-ku# kuḻaṯa palyaṉi#palyaṉi#||
<i>/*My younger brother is sick and tired*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻanypa pikatjara munu paku.||	
<i>/*My younger brother is sick and my older brother is well*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻanypa pikatjara ka ngayuku#ngayulu# kuṯa palya||	
<i>/*My father made a spear and speared a 'roo.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# mama|ngku#-ngku# kuḻaṯa palyaṉu#palyaṉi# munu maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
<i>/*My father speared a 'roo and my son speared an emu.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# mama|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi# ka ngayuku#ngayulu# katja|ngku#-ngku# kaḻaya wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
<i>/*In the following sentences, use short forms:*/</i>||	
<i>/*We two are going to camp.*/</i>|| ngura|kutu#-kutu#|li#ngali# ananyi#ananyi#||	
<i>/*My younger brother hit me.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# maḻany#maḻanypa#|tju#-tju#|ṉi#ngayulu# pungu#punganyi#||	
<i>/*The kangaroo sees you.*/</i>|| maḻu|ngku#-ngku#|nta#nyuntu# nyanganyi#nyanganyi#||	
<i>/*My father made a spear for me.*/</i>|| ngayuku#ngayulu# mama|ngku#-ngku#|tju#ngayulu# kuḻaṯa palyaṉu#palyaṉi#||	
<i>/*THE END*/</i>||

<i>/*The dogs were coming to camp*/</i>||	
Papa tjuṯa ngura|kutu#-kutu# pitjangi#pitjanyi#||

<i>/*The woman with many foods was sitting*/</i>||
Minyma mai tjuṯa|tjara#-tjara# nyinangi#nyinanyi#||

<i>/*The children run from the rocks*/</i>||
Tjitji tjuṯa apu|nguṟu#-nguṟu# wirtjapakalpai#wirtjapakaṉi#||

<i>/*The man with food was hitting the dog*/</i>||	
Wati mai|tjara#-tjara#|ngku#-ngku# papa pungangi#punganyi#||

<i>/*Children go with dogs*/</i>||	
Tjitji tjuṯa papa|tjara#-tjara# ankupai#ananyi#||

<i>/*The woman with many dogs can talk*/</i>||	
Minyma papa tjuṯa|tjara#-tjara# wangkapai#wangkanyi#||

<i>/*The dog runs to camp with the food*/</i>||	
Papa mai|tjara#-tjara# ngura|kutu#-kutu# wirtjapakalpai#wirtjapakaṉi#||

<i>/*The woman is hitting the dog (that has/with the) food*/</i>||	
Minyma|ngku#-ngku# papa mai|tjara#-tjara# punganyi||	

<i>/*The man with the child was falling*/</i>||
Wati tjitji|tjara#-tjara# punkaṉingi#punkaṉi#||	

<i>/*The children were sitting*/</i>||
Tjitji tjuṯa nyinangi#nyinanyi#||

<h2>/*A. Vocabulary*/||</h2>

panya||	<i>/*the one previously referred to, "remember"*/</i>||	
katu||   <i>/*top, high, loud*/</i>||	
piṟuku||   <i>/*again*/</i>||	
maḻaku||   <i>/*(to come) back*/</i>||	
tjarpangu#tjarpanyi#||   <i>/*entered, (of the sun) set*/</i>||

ngula||   <i>/*soon, not yet, later*/</i>||	
anu#ananyi#||	<i>/*went*/</i>||

-ya#tjana#||   <i>/*they (suffix)*/</i>||	
ngananya||   <i>/*who?*/</i>||	
nyaa||   <i>/*what?*/</i>||	
nyaaṉu||	<i>/*did what?*/</i>||	

<h2>/*B. Text*/||</h2>
<b>Nyitayira Tjuṯa Uṟu|ku#-ku# Ankuntja#ananyi#</b>||	
<i>/*The Time the Boys Went to the Water.*/</i>||
Mungaṯu|ya#tjana# nyitayira tjuṯa tangkiyi|tjara#-tjara# anu#ananyi# Itjinpiri#Itjinpiri#|la#-la#|kutu#-kutu# munu|ya#tjana# uṟu|ngka#-ngka# tjarpangu#tjarpanyi#.|| Panya nyara tjana uṟu|ku#-ku# mukuringkupai#mukuringanyi#, munu|ya#tjana# inkangi#inkanyi# uṟu wiṟu|ngka#-ngka# munu|ya#tjana# wararakatingi#wararakatinyi# apu katu|nguṟu#-nguṟu#, munu|ya#tjana# ikaringangi#ikaringanyi#.||
Munu|ya#tjana# ngula pakaṉu#pakaṉi# munu|ya#tjana# tangkiyi|ngka#-ngka# piṟuku tatiṉu#tatiṉi# munu|ya#tjana# anu#ananyi# ngura Tjalyiritja#Tjalyiritja#|la#-la#|kutu#-kutu# munu|ya#tjana# rapita tjawaṉu#tjawaṉi#.|| Ka tjiṟirpi tjarpangu#tjarpanyi# ka|ya#tjana# maḻaku pitjangu#pitjanyi# ngura|kutu#-kutu#, rapita tjuṯa|tjara#-tjara#.||

<i>/*Soon, when he comes, he will go into the wurlie*/</i>||

Mungaṯu minyma tjawaṟa#tjawaṉi# tjawaṟa#tjawaṉi# mai|tjara#-tjara# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|pitjangi#pitjanyi#||	
<i>/*The other day the woman was coming here with food, having dug and dug*/</i>||

Nyitayira tjuṯa pukuḻpa nyinangi#nyinanyi#||
<i>/*The boys were sitting happily*/</i>||

<i>/*Because they were given food, the boys were sitting happily*/</i>||	

Paluṟu paṉa|ngka#-ngka# ngaringi#ngarinyi#||	
<i>/*He was lying on the ground*/</i>||	
Puṉu|nguṟu#-nguṟu# punkara#punkaṉi# paluṟu paṉa|ngka#-ngka# ngaringi#ngarinyi#||
<i>/*Having fallen from the tree, he was lying on the ground*/</i>||

Maḻu punkalpai#punkaṉi#||	
<i>/*Kangaroos fall*/</i>||	
Maḻu punkalpai#punkaṉi# kuḻaṯa|ngka#-ngka# wakanyangka#wakaṉi#||	
<i>/*When pierced with a spear, kangaroos fall*/</i>||	

Tjitji|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wiṟu piṟuku nyangu#nyanganyi#||
<i>/*The child saw the lovely kangaroo again*/</i>||

<i>/*The child saw the lovely kangaroo again as it got up*/</i>||	

Tjana @ma-@#ma-#|nyangu#nyanganyi# tjitji wiṟu tjuṯa||
<i>/*They saw the lovely children.*/</i>||

<i>/*They saw the lovely children playing about*/</i>||

Wati|ngku#-ngku# nyitayira nyangu#nyanganyi# @ma-@#ma-#|ngaṟanyangka#ngaṟanyi#||   @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||	
Wati|ngku#-ngku# nyitayira nyangu#nyanganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   maḻu||	
Wati|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   minyma||
Wati|ngku#-ngku# minyma nyangu#nyanganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   papa||	
Wati|ngku#-ngku# papa nyangu#nyanganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   ungangi#unganyi#||	
Wati|ngku#-ngku# papa ungangi#unganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   tjitji||	
Wati|ngku#-ngku# tjitji ungangi#unganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   nyitayira||	
Wati|ngku#-ngku# nyitayira ungangi#unganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   minyma||	
Wati|ngku#-ngku# minyma ungangi#unganyi# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|wirtjapakanyangka#wirtjapakaṉi#||   mukuringkunyangka#mukuringanyi#||

<h2>/*F. Translate into the language.*/||</h2>
<i>/*While coming frcm camp the men saw a kangaroo*/</i>||	
Ngura|nguṟu#-nguṟu# pitjala#pitjanyi# wati tjuṯa|ngku#-ngku# maḻu nyangu#nyanganyi#||

<i>/*The child speared the dog when it jumped up*/</i>||	
Tjitji|ngku#-ngku# papa wakaṉu#wakaṉi# pakanyangka#pakaṉi#||

<i>/*The other day the women were talking sitting in the shade*/</i>||	
Mungaṯu minyma tjuṯa wangkangi#wangkanyi# wiltja|ngka#-ngka# nyinara#nyinanyi#||

<i>/*The men went away because the children played around*/</i>||	
Wati tjuṯa anu#ananyi# tjitji tjuṯa @para-@#para-#|inkanyangka#inkanyi#||

<i>/*The boy ran away because the man hit him*/</i>||	
Nyitayira @ma-@#ma-#|wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# wati|ngku#-ngku# pungkunyangka#punganyi#||

<i>/*Having come into the wurlie he gave the woman food*/</i>||
Wiltja|ngka#-ngka# tjarpara#tjarpanyi# paluṟu minyma mai ungu#unganyi#||

<i>/*When the woman came into the wurlie he gave her food*/</i>||	
Minyma wiltja|ngka#-ngka# tjarpanyangka#tjarpanyi# paluṟu mai ungu#unganyi#||

<i>/*Having climbed the high mountain the boys came back to camp*/</i>||	
Apu katu tatiṟa#tatiṉi# nyitayira tjuṯa maḻaku pitjangu#pitjanyi# ngura|kutu#-kutu#||

Ngura kutjupa|ngka#-ngka# kunyu tjitji tjuṯa anu#ananyi# mina|ngku#-ngku# puyinyangka#puyiṉi#.|| Tjitji nyara paluṟu tjana waṟu tjaa|tjara#-tjara# anu#ananyi# munu|ya#tjana# ankula#ananyi# ili|kutu#-kutu# pukuḻpa wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# mai ngaṟanyangka#ngaṟanyi#.|| Palu ili nyara paluṟu apu kulpikulpi|ngka#-ngka# unngu ngaṟangi#ngaṟanyi# ka|ya#tjana# tjitji panya tjuṯa|ngku#-ngku# waṟu tjaa uṟil|ta#-ta# wantikatira#wantikatinyi# @ma-@#ma-#|tjarpangu#tjarpanyi# mai panya ili|ku#-ku# munu|ya#tjana# ngalkula#ngalkuṉi# ngalkula#ngalkuṉi# paltjaringkula watjaṉu#watjaṉi# "Wala|la#nganaṉa# pakala#pakaṉi# uṟil|kutu#-kutu#, puyiṉu#puyiṉi#|lanya#nganaṉa#."|| Munu|ya#tjana# pakaṉu#pakaṉi#, wari|ngku#-ngku# puḻkaṟa puyinyangka#puyiṉi#, munu|ya#tjana# pakaṟa#pakaṉi# uṟil|ta#-ta# nyangu#nyanganyi# "Awari waṟu panya yaaltji?|| Mantjila#mantjiṉi#|ya#tjana# wanyu munu puula. Awari puḻkaṟa|ṉi#ngayulu# puyiṉi."|| Palu waṟu ilungu#ilunyi# alatjiṯu ka|ya#tjana# kaṯiṯi tirkiltjingaṉu#tirkiltjingaṉi# alatjiṯu wari|ngku#-ngku# puḻkaṟa puyinyangka#puyiṉi# munu|ya#tjana# wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# ngura|ku#-ku# waṟu|kutu#-kutu#.||

Puṉu|ṉi#ngayulu# uwa#unganyi#, ka|ṉa#ngayulu# papa puḻka pungkuku#punganyi#.||
<i>/*Give me the stick and I'l1 hit the big dog*/</i>||

<i>/*Give me the stick to hit the big dog.*/</i>||

Pakaṉi|ṉa#ngayulu# pulala#pula#, uṟil|kutu#-kutu#, ka|lanya#nganaṉa# mina|ngku#-ngku# puyilku#puyiṉi#||	
<i>/*I am going outside with them and the rain will cool us*/</i>||

<i>/*I going outside with them so that the rain can cool us.*/</i>||

Tjiṟirpi pakanyangka#pakaṉi#|ya#tjana# pitja#pitjanyi#, munu nganaṉala#nganaṉa# maḻu|ku#-ku# ara#ananyi#||	
<i>/*Come when the sun rises and go with us for kangaroo*/</i>||	
Tjiṟirpi pakanyangka#pakaṉi#|ya#tjana# pitja#pitjanyi#, nganaṉala#nganaṉa# maḻu|ku#-ku# ankuntjikitja#ananyi#||
<i>/*Come when the sun rises so that you can go with us for kangaroo*/</i>||

Minyma tjuṯa piti|tjara#-tjara#|ngku#-ngku# ili mantjiningi#mantjiṉi#||	
<i>/*The women with dishes are getting figs*/</i>||	
Minyma tjuṯa piti|tjara#-tjara#|ngku#-ngku# ili mantjiningi#mantjiṉi# ngalkuntjikitja#ngalkuṉi#|ngku#-ngku#||
<i>/*The women with dishes are getting figs to eat*/</i>||

Kuḻaṯa tjukutjuku tjuṯa|ya#tjana# mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi#||	
<i>/*They got little spears*/</i>||
Kuḻaṯa tjukutjuku tjuṯa|ya#tjana# mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi# mai wakantjikitja#wakaṉi#|ngku#-ngku#||
<i>/*They got little spears to pierce the food*/</i>||

Tjitji tjuṯa|ngku#-ngku# mai tjawalpai#tjawaṉi#, munu|ya#tjana# minyma tjuṯa ungkupai#unganyi#||	
<i>/*The children dig (for) food and give it to the women*/</i>||	
Tjitji tjuṯa|ngku#-ngku# mai tjawalpai#tjawaṉi# minyma tjuṯa ungkuntjikitja#unganyi#|ngku#-ngku#||
<i>/*The children dig food to give to the women*/</i>||

Maḻu pikatjara @ma-@#ma-#|wirtjapakaṉi||	
<i>/*The sick kangaroo is running away*/</i>||	
Maḻu pikatjara @ma-@#ma-#|wirtjapakaṉi iluntjikitja#ilunyi#||
<i>/*The sick kangaroo is running away to die*/</i>||

Nyitayira tjuṯa tangkiyi|tjara#-tjara# anu#ananyi#||	
<i>/*The boys are going on donkeys*/</i>||

Wiltja|ngka#-ngka# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|tjarpa#tjarpanyi#, nganaṉala#nganaṉa# ngalkuntjikitja#ngalkuṉi#||

/*5.*/|| <i>/*The man was running with a stick to hit that child*/</i>||
Wati puṉu|tjara#-tjara# wirtjapakaṉingi#wirtjapakaṉi# tjitji nyara pungkuntjikitja#punganyi#||

/*6.*/|| <i>/*The children came back to camp to give us food*/</i>||

wangkangu#wangkanyi#|linya#ngali#||   <i>/*spoke with us (2)*/</i>||	
wangkangu#wangkanyi#|lanya#nganaṉa#||   <i>/*spoke with us (all)*/</i>||	
wangkangu#wangkanyi#|nta#nyuntu#||	<i>/*spoke with you*/</i>||	
wangkangu#wangkanyi#|lta#paluṟu#||   <i>/*spoke with him*/</i>||	
<h2>/*C. Sentences.*/||</h2> 
<i>/*Now you will hear a sentence using only known items, and following	
it, one using the items introduced in Part A of this unit.	
Listen and repeat.*/</i>||	
/*1.*/|| Kungka uwankara|ya#tjana# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# pitja#pitjanyi#, mai|ku#-ku#||	
Kungka uwankara|ya#tjana# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# pitjama#pitjanyi# mai|ku#-ku#||	
/*2.*/|| Tjiṟirpi pakanyangka#pakaṉi# pula pitjala#pitjanyi# kuḻaṯa panya mantjila#mantjiṉi#||	
Tjiṟirpi pakanyangka#pakaṉi# pula pitjala#pitjanyi# kuḻaṯa panyanpa mantjinma#mantjiṉi#||	
/*3.*/|| Tjitji langka nyara witila#witiṉi# urinyangka#urinyi#||	
Tjitji langka nyara witinma#witiṉi# urinyangka#urinyi#||	
/*4.*/|| Uwankara|ya#tjana# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulila#kulini# ka|lanya#nganaṉa# wangkaku#wangkanyi#||
Uwankara|ya#tjana# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulinma#kulini# ka|lanya#nganaṉa# wangkaku#wangkanyi#||
/*5.*/|| Minyma, waḻi|ngka#-ngka# nyinara#nyinanyi# ngangkaḻi nyawa#nyanganyi# ulpuru kuḻu||	
Minyma, waḻi|ngka#-ngka# nyinara#nyinanyi# ngangkaḻi nyangama#nyanganyi# ulpuru kuḻu||	
/*6.*/|| Wati tjitji nyuntumpa#nyuntu# mai uwa#unganyi# ngalkuntja#ngalkuṉi#|ku#-ku#||	
Wati tjitji nyuntumpa#nyuntu# mai titutjara|ngku#-ngku# ungama#unganyi# ngalkuntja#ngalkuṉi#|ku#-ku#||	
/*7.*/|| Mungartjirinyangka#mungarinyi# ngura|ngka#-ngka#|linya#ngali# inka#inkanyi#||	
Mungartjirinyangka#mungarinyi# ngura|ngka#-ngka#|linya#ngali# inkama#inkanyi#||	
/*8.*/|| @Ma-@#ma-#|nyawa#nyanganyi#|ya#tjana#, tatiṉu#tatiṉi#|lta#paluṟu# waṟu|tjara#-tjara#||	
@Ma-@#ma-#|nyangama#nyanganyi#|ya#tjana#, tatiṉu#tatiṉi#|lta#paluṟu# waṟu|tjara#-tjara#||	
<h2>/*D. Now listen and repeat these sentences with their English equivalents.*/||</h2>	
Kungka uwankara|ya#tjana# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# pitja#pitjanyi#, mai|ku#-ku#||
<i>/*All the girls come to the house for food*/</i>||	
Kungka uwankara|ya#tjana# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# pitjama#pitjanyi# mai|ku#-ku#||	
<i>/*All the girls keep coming to the house for food*/</i>||

Tjiṟirpi pakanyangka#pakaṉi# pula pitjala#pitjanyi# kuḻaṯa panyanpa mantjila#mantjiṉi#||	
<i>/*When the sun rises come get those spears*/</i>||	
Tjiṟirpi pakanyangka#pakaṉi# pula pitjala#pitjanyi# kuḻaṯa panyanpa mantjinma#mantjiṉi#||	
<i>/*When the sun rises keep coming to get those spears*/</i>||

Tjitji langka nyara witila#witiṉi# urinyangka#urinyi#||	
<i>/*Child, when the lizard moves, grab it*/</i>||	
Tjitji langka nyara witinma#witiṉi# urinyangka#urinyi#||	
<i>/*Child, when the lizard moves, keep on holding it*/</i>||

Uwankara|ya#tjana# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulila#kulini# ka|lanya#nganaṉa# wangkaku#wangkanyi#||
<i>/*All of you listen here so that he can speak with us*/</i>||	
Uwankara|ya#tjana# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulinma#kulini# ka|lanya#nganaṉa# wangkaku#wangkanyi#||
<i>/*All of you keep listening here so that he ean speak with us*/</i>||

Minyma, waḻi|ngka#-ngka# nyinara#nyinanyi# ngangkaḻi nyawa#nyanganyi# ulpuru kuḻu||
<i>/*Woman, while in the house, look at the clouds, the dust too*/</i>||
Minyma, waḻi|ngka#-ngka# nyinara#nyinanyi# ngangkaḻi nyangama#nyanganyi# ulpuru kuḻu||
<i>/*Woman, while in the house, keep looking at the clouds, the dust too*/</i>||

Wati tjitji nyuntumpa#nyuntu# mai uwa#unganyi# ngalkuntja#ngalkuṉi#|ku#-ku#||		
<i>/*Man, give your child food to eat*/</i>||	
Wati tjitji nyuntumpa#nyuntu# mai titutjara|ngku#-ngku# ungama#unganyi# ngalkuntja#ngalkuṉi#|ku#-ku#||		
<i>/*Man, always give your child food to eat*/</i>||

Mungartjirinyangka#mungarinyi# ngura|ngka#-ngka#|linya#ngali# inka#inkanyi#||	
<i>/*When it's night sing with us (2) in camp*/</i>||	
Mungartjirinyangka#mungarinyi# ngura|ngka#-ngka#|linya#ngali# inkama#inkanyi#||
<i>/*When it's night keep singing with us in camp*/</i>||

@Ma-@#ma-#|nyawa#nyanganyi#|ya#tjana#, tatiṉu#tatiṉi#|lta#paluṟu# waṟu|tjara#-tjara#||	
<i>/*Look there, he has climbed it, with fire*/</i>||	
@Ma-@#ma-#|nyangama#nyanganyi#|ya#tjana#, tatiṉu#tatiṉi#|lta#paluṟu# waṟu|tjara#-tjara#||	
<i>/*Keep looking there, he has climbed it, with fire*/</i>||

<h2>/*F. Translate into the language.*/||</h2>
<i>/*Children, always come back to camp, at night*/</i>||	
Tjitji tjuṯa titutjara ngura|kutu#-kutu# maḻaku pitjama#pitjanyi# munga|ngka#-ngka#||

<i>/*Woman, get the lizard with us two*/</i>||	
Minyma langka|linya#ngali# mantjila#mantjiṉi#||

<i>/*Children keep on eating the figs when you've collected them*/</i>||	
Tjitji tjuṯa ili ngalkunma, uraṟa#uraṉi#||

<i>/*When it rains everyone keep on galloping for camp and I'll stay here with him*/</i>||
Mina|ngku#-ngku# puyinyangka#puyiṉi# ngura|ku#-ku#|ya#tjana# uwankara wirtjapakanma#wirtjapakaṉi# ka ngayulu nyanga|ngka#-ngka# nyinaku#nyinanyi# palula#paluṟu#||

<i>/*When the dust comes, don't be afraid*/</i>||	
Ulpuru pakanyangka#pakaṉi#|ya#tjana# nguḻu|wiya nyinama#nyinanyi#||

<i>/*Keep spearing the kangaroo so it will die*/</i>||	
Maḻu wakanma#wakaṉi# iluntja#ilunyi#|ku#-ku#||

<i>/*Oh dear, let us keep running very quickly, the cold is chilling us*/</i>||	
Awari, wala puḻka mulapa|la#nganaṉa# wirtjapakanma#wirtjapakaṉi#, wari|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# puyiṉi||

<i>/*I am afraid, let us enter the wurlie again*/</i>||	
Ngayulu nguḻu, wanyu|la#nganaṉa# wiltja|ngka#-ngka# piṟuku tjarpa#tjarpanyi#||

<i>/*Having climbed the hill, look at the big clouds*/</i>||	
Apu|ngka#-ngka#|ya#tjana# tatiṟa#tatiṉi# ngangkaḻi puḻka nyangama#nyanganyi#||

<h2>/*B. Text.*/||</h2>	
<b>Tjamu|ku#-ku# Wiltjantja#wiltjaṉi#</b>||	
Ngura kutjupa|ngka#-ngka#|ya#tjana# kunyu tjitji kungka maṉkurpa#maṉkur# nyinangi#nyinanyi# ka tjiṟirpi kutjupa ngangkaḻi puḻka ngaṟangi#ngaṟanyi# ilkari|ngka#-ngka# mina|tjara#-tjara# munu puyiningi#puyiṉi#|lta#paluṟu# iili|ngku#-ngku#.|| Ka|ya#tjana# kunyu tjitji panya kungka maṉkur|tu#-tu# wiltjantjikitjangku#wiltjaṉi# kulinu#kulini# iili|ngka#-ngka# tawara#-tawara#, munu|ya#tjana# tjiṟirpi nyara palula#paluṟu# wiltjaṉingi#wiltjaṉi# iili unngu-unngu wiltja tjanampa#tjana# warara.|| Munu|ya#tjana# nyangu#nyanganyi# wati tjilpi tjanampa#tjana# tjamu nyinanyangka#nyinanyi# munu|ya#tjana# wiltjaṉu#wiltjaṉi# palumpa#paluṟu#, wiltja puḻka munu|ya#tjana# untjuntju tjunangi#tjunanyi# wiltja|ngka#-ngka# katu ka wiltja wiṟu ngaṟangi#ngaṟanyi# wati panya tjilpi|ku#-ku#.|| Ka|ya#tjana# wiltjara#wiltjaṉi# wiyaringkula#wiyarinyi# mungaringkunyangka#mungarinyi# ankula#ananyi# kunkunaringu#kunkunarinyi#.||
Palu munga|ngka#-ngka# iili|ngku#-ngku# rawa|ngku#-ngku# puyiningi#puyiṉi# ka|ya#tjana# tjitji panya kungka maṉkurpa#maṉkur# kunkunaringu#kunkunarinyi# tjamu|ku#-ku# ngura|ngka#-ngka# itingka munu|ya#tjana# watarku ngaringi#ngarinyi#.|| Ka ngula, munga kultu|ngka#-ngka# wati panya tjilpi|ku#-ku# wiltja pilukatingu#pilukatinyi# ka tjilpi panya ngaltutjara|ngku#-ngku# kunkunpa puḻkatjanungku	urulyarara#urulyaraṉi# pakaṟa#pakaṉi# puṯu pakaṉu#pakaṉi# palu wiltja pilukatingu#pilukatinyi# alatjiṯu ka tjamu|ngku#-ngku# watjaṉu#watjaṉi# "Puḻiri pitjala#pitjanyi#|ya#tjana# katula#katuṉi#, wiltja nyanga pilukatingu#pilukatinyi#."|| Ka|ya#tjana# kunyu puḻiri maṉkurpa#maṉkur# pakaṟa#pakaṉi# wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# munu|ya#tjana# kunyu manyirka	ankula#ananyi# kutju puḻkaṟa urinyangka#urinyi# nyangu#nyanganyi# munu|ya#tjana# puṉu mantjira#mantjiṉi# waṉi-waṉingu#waṉinyi# ka wankaṯu pupangi#pupanyi#.|| Ka|ya#tjana# mantjira#mantjiṉi# wiltja tjanama|ngka#-ngka# tjunu#tjunanyi# ka ngaringi#ngarinyi# tjamu panya tjanampa#tjana#.||

<h2>/*D. Questions*/||</h2>	
/*1.*/|| Kungka maṉkur|tu#-tu# nyaantjikitjangku kulinu#kulini#, iili|ngku#-ngku# puyinyangka#puyiṉi#?||	
Wiltjantjikitjangku#wiltjaṉi#|ya#tjana# kulinu#kulini#, iili|ngka#-ngka# tawara#-tawara#.||

/*2.*/|| Munu|ya#tjana# wiltjara#wiltjaṉi# ngananya nyangu#nyanganyi#, nyinanyangka#nyinanyi#?||	
Tjanampa#tjana# tjamu nyangu#nyanganyi#, kungka maṉkur|tu#-tu#.||

/*3.*/|| Munu|ya#tjana# nyakula#nyinanyi# nyaaṉu palumpa#paluṟu#?||	
Wiltjaṉu#wiltjaṉi#|ya#tjana# piṟuku, palumpa#paluṟu#.||

/*4.*/|| Wiltja wiṟu wanyu?||
Uwa#unganyi#, wiltja wiṟu, puḻka mulapa, untjuntju tjuṯa|tjara#-tjara#.||

/*5.*/|| Ka|ya#tjana# wiltjara#wiltjaṉi# wiyaringkula#wiyarinyi# nyaaringu#nyaaringanyi#?||
Ankula#ananyi#|ya#tjana# kunkunaringu#kunkunarinyi# tjanama|ngka#-ngka#.||

/*6.*/|| Ka munga|ngka#-ngka#, tjamu|ngku#-ngku# nyaaku watjaṉu#watjaṉi# pitjantja#pitjanyi#|ku#-ku#?||	
Palumpa#paluṟu# wiltja pilukatinyangka#pilukatinyi#.||

/*7.*/|| Munu paluṟu, tjamu panya, yaaltji ngaringi#ngarinyi#?||	
Paluṟu unngu ngaringi#ngarinyi# ka wiltja pilukatingu#pilukatinyi# alatjiṯu.||

/*8.*/|| Awari kungka maṉkur|tu#-tu# nyaaṉu?||	
Pakaṟa#pakaṉi#|ya#tjana#, wirtjapakara#wirtjapakaṉi# waṉi-waṉingu#waṉinyi# untjuntju munu|ya#tjana# tjilpi mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi#.||

/*9.*/|| Munu|ya#tjana# yaaltji|ngka#-ngka# palunya#paluṟu# tjunu#tjunanyi# kunkunarintja|ku#-ku#?||	
Wiltja tjanama|ngka#-ngka#|ya#tjana# tjunu#tjunanyi#, paluṟu ngaltutjara kunkunarintja|ku#-ku#.||

/*10.*/|| Nyuntu wanyu mukuringu#mukuringanyi# story nyanga|ku#-ku#?||	
Uwa ngayulu mukuringu#mukuringanyi#. Story wiṟu nyangatja.||

ungkuwiya#unganyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of give*/</i>||
nyakuwiya#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of look, see*/</i>||
ankuwiya#ananyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of go*/</i>||
wirkankuwiya#wirkananyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of arrive*/</i>||
pitjawiyangku#pitjanyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of come*/</i>||	
wangkawiyangku#wangkanyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of talk*/</i>||
wakalwiyangku#wakaṉi#||   <i>/*Negative form of pierce*/</i>||
wirtjapakalwiyangku#wirtjapakaṉi#||   <i>/*Negative form of run*/</i>||
ungkuwiyangku#unganyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of give*/</i>||	
nyakuwiyangku#nyanganyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of look, see*/</i>||	
ankuwiyangku#ananyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of go*/</i>||	
wirkankuwiyangku#wirkananyi#||   <i>/*Negative form of arrive*/</i>||	
wanti#wantinyi#||   <i>/*avoid*/</i>||
wantima#wantinyi#||   <i>/*keep on avoiding*/</i>||
wantinyi||   <i>/*is avoiding*/</i>||	
wantipai#wantinyi#||   <i>/*avoids*/</i>||	
wantingu#wantinyi#||   <i>/*avoided*/</i>||	
wantingi#wantinyi#||   <i>/*was avoiding*/</i>||	
wantiku#wantinyi#||   <i>/*will avoid*/</i>||
nyinantja#nyinanyi#||   <i>/*the one who is sitting*/</i>||	
nyinantjitja#nyinanyi#||   <i>/*the one who is sitting*/</i>||	
punkantja#punkaṉi#||   <i>/*the one who is falling, or who fell*/</i>||	
punkantjitja#punkaṉi#||   <i>/*the one who is falling, or who fell*/</i>||
pungkuntja#punganyi#||   <i>/*the one who is hitting, or who was hit*/</i>||	
pungkuntjitja#punganyi#||   <i>/*the one who is hitting, or who was hit*/</i>||	
tjunkuntja#tjunanyi#||   <i>/*the one that is put, was put*/</i>||	
tjunkuntjitja#tjunanyi#||   <i>/*the one that is put, was put*/</i>||	
<h2>/*C. Now you will hear a sentence you know and following it, the same one incorporating a negative.*/||</h2> 
<i>/*Listen and repeat:*/</i>||	
Tjilpi tjuṯa watarku nyinanyi||	
Tjilpi tjuṯa pitjawiya#pitjanyi# watarku nyinanyi||

Ngayuku#ngayulu# tjamu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
Ngayuku#ngayulu# tjamu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakalwiyangku#wakaṉi# wantingu#wantinyi#||

Kungka tjuṯa @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulinma#kulini#|ya#tjana#||	
Kungka tjuṯa, para|nyakuwiyangku#nyanganyi#|ya#tjana# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulinma#kulini#||

Tjitji nyara|ngku#-ngku# mai wiṟu waṉipai#waṉinyi#||	
Tjitji nyara|ngku#-ngku# mai wiṟu waṉipai#waṉinyi# ngalkuwiyangku#ngalkuṉi#||

Tjitji punkantja#punkaṉi# pitjanyi||	
Tjitji punkantja#punkaṉi# wirtjapakalwiya#wirtjapakaṉi# pitjanyi||

Wati pungkuntja#punganyi#|lu#-lu# kuḻaṯa mantjiṉi wakantjikitjangu#wakaṉi#||	
Wati pungkuntja#punganyi#|lu#-lu# kuḻaṯa waṉinyi wakalwiyangku#wakaṉi#||

Wanyu, mai piti|ngka#-ngka# tjunkuntja#tjunanyi# mantjila#mantjiṉi#||	
Wanyu, mai piti|ngka#-ngka# tjunkuntjitja#tjunanyi# mantjilwiyangku#mantjiṉi# wantima#wantinyi#||	

Tjilpi panya wakantja#wakaṉi# ngarinyi||	
Tjilpi panya wakantja#wakaṉi# ngalkuwiya#ngalkuṉi# ngarinyi||

Minyma pungkuntjitjangku#punganyi# palunya#paluṟu# ungkuku#unganyi#||	
Minyma pungkuntjitjangku#punganyi# palunya#paluṟu# ungkuwiyangku#unganyi# wantiku#wantinyi#||	
<h2>/*D. Now the same sentences again with their English equivalents.*/||</h2> 
Tjilpi tjuṯa watarku nyinanyi||
<i>/*The old men are oblivious*/</i>||
Tjilpi tjuṯa pitjawiya#pitjanyi# watarku nyinanyi||
<i>/*The old men are not coming, they are oblivious*/</i>||

Ngayuku#ngayulu# tjamu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
<i>/*My grandfather speared a kangaroo*/</i>||
Ngayuku#ngayulu# tjamu|ngku#-ngku# maḻu wakalwiyangku#wakaṉi# wantingu#wantinyi#||
<i>/*My grandfather didn't spear a kangaroo*/</i>||

Kungka tjuṯa @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulinma#kulini#|ya#tjana#||	
<i>/*Girls, listen here*/</i>||
Kungka tjuṯa, para|nyakuwiyangku#nyanganyi#|ya#tjana# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kulinma#kulini#||
<i>/*Girls, @don't@ look around, listen here*/</i>||

Tjitji nyara|ngku#-ngku# mai wiṟu waṉipai#waṉinyi#||	
<i>/*That child throws away good food*/</i>||
Tjitji nyara|ngku#-ngku# mai wiṟu waṉipai#waṉinyi# ngalkuwiyangku#ngalkuṉi#||
<i>/*That child @doesn't@ eat the good food, he throws it away*/</i>||	

Tjitji punkantja#punkaṉi# pitjanyi||	
<i>/*The child who fell is coming*/</i>||
Tjitji punkantja#punkaṉi# wirtjapakalwiya#wirtjapakaṉi# pitjanyi||
<i>/*The child who fell is not running*/</i>||	

Wati pungkuntja#punganyi#|lu#-lu# kuḻaṯa waṉinyi wakalwiyangku#wakaṉi#||
<i>/*[The sentence above is wrong]. The man who was hit is getting the spear to spear him*/</i>||
Wati pungkuntja#punganyi#|lu#-lu# kuḻaṯa waṉinyi wakalwiyangku#wakaṉi#||
<i>/*The man who was hit is not spearing him but throwing away the spear*/</i>||	

Wanyu, mai piti|ngka#-ngka# tjunkuntjitja#tjunanyi# mantjila#mantjiṉi#||	
<i>/*Wait get the food that was put in the dish*/</i>||
Wanyu, mai piti|ngka#-ngka# tjunkuntjitja#tjunanyi# mantjilwiyangku#mantjiṉi# wantima#wantinyi#||	
<i>/*Wait, don't get the food that was put in the dish*/</i>||	

Tjilpi panya wakantja#wakaṉi# ngarinyi||	
<i>/*The old man who was speared, remember is lying down*/</i>||
Tjilpi panya wakantja#wakaṉi# ngalkuwiya#ngalkuṉi# ngarinyi||
<i>/*The old man who was speared is not eating*/</i>||

Minyma pungkuntjitjangku#punganyi# palunya#paluṟu# ungkuku#unganyi#||	
<i>/*The woman who was hit will give it him*/</i>||
Minyma pungkuntjitjangku#punganyi# palunya#paluṟu# ungkuwiyangku#unganyi# wantiku#wantinyi#||	
<i>/*The woman who was hit won't give to him*/</i>||	

<h2>/*E. Now a 4 Phase Drill.*/||</h2> 
<i>/*You will hear a sentence followed by a cue, use this cue to make a new sentence. Off you go:*/</i>||	
Minyma pungkuntja#punganyi#|la#nganaṉa# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   wati||	
Wati pungkuntja#punganyi#|la#nganaṉa# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   tjitji||	
Tjitji pungkuntja#punganyi#|la#nganaṉa# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   nyitayira||	
Nyitayira pungkuntja#punganyi#|la#nganaṉa# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   tjilpi||	
Tjilpi pungkuntja#punganyi#|la#nganaṉa# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   kungka||	
Kungka pungkuntja#punganyi#|la#nganaṉa# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   tatintja#tatiṉi#|lu#-lu#||	
Kungka tatintja#tatiṉi#|lu#-lu# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   wati||	
Wati tatintja#tatiṉi#|lu#-lu# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   minyma||	
Minyma tatintja#tatiṉi#|lu#-lu# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   nyitayira||	
Nyitayira tatintja#tatiṉi#|lu#-lu# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   tjilpi||	
Tjilpi tatintja#tatiṉi#|lu#-lu# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||   tjitji||	
Tjitji tatintja#tatiṉi#|lu#-lu# wiltjalwiyangku#wiltjaṉi# wantinyi||

<h2>/*F. Translate into Pitjantjatjara*/||</h2> 	
/*1.*/|| <i>/*Grandfather, don't go out for kangaroo*/</i>||	
Tjamu, maḻu|ku#-ku# ankuwiya#ananyi# nyinama#nyinanyi#||

/*2.*/|| <i>/*He didn't like the food*/</i>||	
Paluṟu mai mukuringkuwiyangku#mukuringanyi# wantingu#wantinyi#||	

/*3.*/|| <i>/*The speared kangaroo didn't die*/</i>||	
Maḻu wakantja#wakaṉi# iluwiya#ilunyi# @ma-@#ma-#|wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#||

/*4.*/|| <i>/*The woman who's been hit won't eat*/</i>||	
Minyma pungkuntja#punganyi#|lu#-lu# ngalkuwiyangku#ngalkuṉi# wantinyi||	

/*5.*/|| <i>/*The man with many dogs doesn't give his children food*/</i>||	
Wati papa tjuṯa|tjara#-tjara#|ngku#-ngku# palumpa#paluṟu# tjitji mai ungkuwiyangku#unganyi# wantipai#wantinyi#||

/*6.*/|| <i>/*The men who arrived the other day are not singing*/</i>||	
Wati mungaṯu wirkankuntjitja#wirkananyi# tjuṯa inkanwiya#inkanyi# nyinanyi||

/*7.*/|| <i>/*Boys, don't throw stones into the water*/</i>||	
Nyitayira tjuṯa, apu uṟu|ngka#-ngka# waniwiyangku#waṉinyi#|ya#tjana# wantima#wantinyi#||

/*8.*/|| <i>/*Why didn't you (all) come with us to climb the mountain?*/</i>||	
Nyaaku nyura nganaṉala#nganaṉa# apu|ngka#-ngka# tatintjikitjangku#tatiṉi# pitjawiyangku#pitjanyi# wantingu#wantinyi#?||

/*9.*/|| <i>/*The three girls didn't dig (for) food*/</i>||	
Kungka maṉkur|tu#-tu# mai tjawaliyangku#tjawaṉi# wantingu#wantinyi#||

/*10.*/|| <i>/*We aren't getting the figs because it's raining*/</i>||	
Nganaṉa ili mantjiliyangku#mantjiṉi# wantinyi, mina|ngku#-ngku# puyinyangka#puyiṉi#||

<h2>/*A. Vocabulary*/||</h2>
kami||   <i>/*grandmother*/</i>||	
nyiiṉka||   <i>/*adolescent boy*/</i>||	
pakaḻi||   <i>/*grandson*/</i>||	
uṉa||   <i>/*rotten, stinking, stench*/</i>||	
pampa||   <i>/*old woman*/</i>||	
kura||   <i>/*bad, naughty*/</i>||	
mungawinki||   <i>/*morning*/</i>||	
kuwari||   <i>/*now*/</i>||	
wiyangka||   <i>/*without*/</i>||	
katingu#katinyi#||   <i>/*took, brought*/</i>||	
uṉaringu#uṉaringanyi#||   <i>/*became rotten, stinking*/</i>||	
pauntjaku#pauṉi#||   <i>/*to cook, so that he could cook*/</i>||	
kanyiningi#kanyiṉi#||   <i>/*was keeping, minding*/</i>||
wiyaringangi#wiyaringanyi#||   <i>/*was finishing*/</i>||	
tjapiningi#tjapini#||   <i>/*was asking*/</i>||	
<h2>/*B. Text*/||</h2>
<b>Kami|ṟara#-ṟara# Pula Iili|ngka#-ngka# Nyinantja#nyinanyi#</b>||	
<i>/*Grandmother and Grandson in the Rain*/</i>||	
Minyma pampa kunyu nyinangi#nyinanyi# kami, ka tjitji nyiiṉka patu nyinangi#nyinanyi#, palumpa#paluṟu# pakaḻi.|| Palu pakaḻi kunyu maḻu|ku#-ku# anu#ananyi# munu ankula#ananyi# iili puḻka|ngka#-ngka#, mina puḻka|ngku#-ngku# puyinyangka#puyiṉi# maḻu pungu#punganyi# munu ngura|kutu#-kutu# katingu#katinyi# munu kami|ngka#-ngka# watjaṉu#watjaṉi#, "Kami waṟu|tju#ngayulu# waṉi#waṉinyi# maḻu pauntjaku#pauṉi#."|| Ka kunyu kami|ngku#-ngku# waṟu waṉingu#waṉinyi# uṟu|ngka#-ngka# ka waṟu ilura#ilunyi# wiyaringu#wiyarinyi#.|| Ka pakaḻi panya paluṟu iili puḻka|ngka#-ngka# waṟu wiya munga|ngka#-ngka# maḻu tjunkula#tjunanyi# ngaringi#ngarinyi#, palu kami waṟu puḻka tjunkula#tjunanyi# wiltja puḻka|ngka#-ngka# ngaringi#ngarinyi#.|| Ka kunyu pakaḻi mungawinki ngarira#ngarinyi# tjiṟirpirira#tjiṟirpirinyi# piṟuku maḻu kutjupa|ku#-ku# anu#ananyi# munu kunyu maḻu watarkurira#watarkurinyi# tulyku|ngka#-ngka# pungu#punganyi# munu pungkula#punganyi# maḻaku|ngku#-ngku# katingu#katinyi# ngura|kutu#-kutu#.|| Palu piṟuku kunyu watjaṉu#watjaṉi#, "Kami, waṟu|tju#ngayulu# waṉi#waṉinyi# maḻu pauntjaku#pauṉi#, maḻu kuwari nyanga kutjupa, panya nganmany#nganmanpa#|tju#ngayulu# pungkuntja#punganyi# uṉaringu#uṉaringanyi# palu kuwari|ṉa#ngayulu# piṟuku pungu#punganyi#, ka palumpa#paluṟu# waṟu waṉi#waṉinyi#."|| Ka waṟu waṉingu#waṉinyi# palu piṟuku ilungu#ilunyi# uṟu|ngka#-ngka#.||
Uwankara kunyu paṉa tulykuringu#tulykurinyi# munu mina puḻkaringu#puḻkarinyi# paṉa|ngka#-ngka# ka paluṟu wiltja kurakura|ngka#-ngka# nyinangi#nyinanyi#, nyiiṉka panya, ka kami wiltja wiṟu|ngka#-ngka# nyinangi#nyinanyi# waṟu|tjara#-tjara#.|| Palu rawa|ngku#-ngku# kunyu maḻu pungangi#punganyi# munu kuwari wiltja panya palumpa#paluṟu#|ngka#-ngka# maḻu uṉaringu#uṉaringanyi# pauntja#pauṉi# wiyangka, ngalkuntja#ngalkuṉi# wiyangka, ka nyiiṉka panya paluṟu puḻkaṟa paṉṯiningi#paṉṯini# uṉa munu kutjupa tjuṯa katira#katinyi# waṉingi#waṉinyi# panya nganmanyitja tjuṯa munu kuwaritja tjuṯa kanyiningi#kanyiṉi# panya pulangkita wiya|ngku#-ngku# palunya#paluṟu# untjunmankuntjaku#untjunmananyi#, waṟu wiyangka.|| Palu kami|ngku#-ngku# kunyu palunya#paluṟu# ungkuwiyangku#unganyi# wantingu#wantinyi#, puṯu kunyu helpamilaningi#helpamilaninyi# waṟu ungkula#unganyi#.|| Waṟu kunyu waṉingi#waṉinyi# ka kunyu mina|ngku#-ngku# wiyaṉingi#wiyaṉi#, iili puḻka|ngku#-ngku#.|| Munu kunyu piṟuku mungawinki kutjupa anu#ananyi# munu maḻu rawa|ngku#-ngku# pungangi#punganyi# munu katira#katinyi# ngura|ngka#-ngka# tjunangi#tjunanyi# palu pauṟa#pauṉi# ngalkuwiya#ngalkuṉi# kunyu waṟu wiya munu kami|ngka#-ngka# rawa|ngku#-ngku# tjapiningi#tjapini#, "Kami waṟu waṉi#waṉinyi# maḻu pauntjaku#pauṉi#."|| Ka kunyu waṟu tjukutjuku rawa|ngku#-ngku# ungangi#unganyi# kami|ngku#-ngku# panya, pakaḻi, ka wiyaringangi#wiyaringanyi#.||

<i>/*[The dictation, repeat (Unit 26)]*/</i>||
<h2>/*D. Questions:*/||</h2>	
/*1.*/|| Ngananya pula nyinangi#nyinanyi#?||	
Minyma pampa kunyu, palumpa#paluṟu# pakaḻi kuḻu nyinangi#nyinanyi#.||
Ngananya pula nyinangi#nyinanyi#?||	

/*2.*/|| Ka nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# nyaaningi rawa|ngku#-ngku#?||	
Paluṟu maḻu|ku#-ku# anangi#ananyi#.||
Ka nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# nyaaningi rawa|ngku#-ngku#?||	

/*3.*/|| Ka waṟu tjaa|tjara#-tjara# nyaaku ilungi#ilunyi# kami|ngku#-ngku# waṉinyangka#waṉinyi#?||	
Uṟu|ngka#-ngka# punkara#punkaṉi# waṟu ilungi#ilunyi#.||
Ka waṟu tjaa|tjara#-tjara# nyaaku ilungi#ilunyi# kami|ngku#-ngku# waṉinyangka#waṉinyi#?||	

/*4.*/|| Ka ngananya wari mulapa ngaringi#ngarinyi# munga|ngka#-ngka#?||	
Nyiiṉka panya wari mulapa ngaringi#ngarinyi# munga|ngka#-ngka#, waṟu wiya, pulangkita|wiya.||
Ka ngananya wari mulapa ngaringi#ngarinyi# munga|ngka#-ngka#?||	

/*5.*/|| Ka nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# maḻu tjuṯa katira#katinyi# tjunkunyangka#tjunanyi# nyaaringangi#nyaaringanyi#?||	
Maḻu tjuṯa uṉaringangi#uṉaringanyi# palumpa#paluṟu# ngura|ngka#-ngka#.||
Ka nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# maḻu tjuṯa katira#katinyi# tjunkunyangka#tjunanyi# nyaaringangi#nyaaringanyi#?||	

/*6.*/|| Ka kami|ngku#-ngku# palunya#paluṟu# nyaa|ku#-ku# puṯu helpamilaṉu?||	
Waṟu tjaa|tjara#-tjara# uṟu|ngka#-ngka# rawa punkanyangka#punkaṉi# kami|ngku#-ngku# puṯu helpamilaṉu.||
Ka kami|ngku#-ngku# palunya#paluṟu# nyaa|ku#-ku# puṯu helpamilaṉu?||	

/*7.*/|| Palumpa#paluṟu# pakaḻi nyaaku waṟu|ku#-ku# mukuringu#mukuringanyi#?||	
Pakaḻi maḻu pauntjikitja#pauṉi# waṟu|ku#-ku# mukuringu#mukuringanyi#.||
Palumpa#paluṟu# pakaḻi nyaaku waṟu|ku#-ku# mukuringu#mukuringanyi#?||	

/*8.*/|| Nyaaku nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# wiltja kami|ku#-ku#|ngka#-ngka# waṟu mantjintikitjangku#mantjiṉi# tjarpawiyangku#tjarpanyi# wantingu#wantinyi#?||	
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# panya minyma wantipai#wantinyi#.||
Nyaaku nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# wiltja kami|ku#-ku#|ngka#-ngka# waṟu mantjintikitjangku#mantjiṉi# tjarpawiyangku#tjarpanyi# wantingu#wantinyi#?||	

<h2>/*E. Learn the first two sentences of the story by heart.*/||</h2>	

<i>/*End of Unit 26.*/</i>||

<h2>/*B. Now listen again to the same words fixing the English meanings in your mind.*/||</h2> 
<i>/*Off you go.*/</i>||	
waṉintjaku#waṉinyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so that he won't throw it*/</i>||	
katintjaku#katinyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so that he won't take it*/</i>||	
punkantjaku#punkaṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so that he won't fall*/</i>||	
mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so that he won't get it*/</i>||	
pungkuntjaku#punganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so he won't hit it*/</i>||	
nyakuntjaku#nyanganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so that he won't see it*/</i>||	
ankuntjaku#ananyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so that he won't go*/</i>||
tjunkuntjaku#tjunanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   <i>/*so that he won't put it*/</i>||	
ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu#||   <i>/*I, myself*/</i>||	
nyuntu|nku#-nku#||   <i>/*you, yourself*/</i>||	
paluṟu|nku#-nku#||   <i>/*he, himself*/</i>||	
ngali|nku#-nku#||   <i>/*we two, ourselves*/</i>||	
nyupali|nku#-nku#||   <i>/*you two, yourselves*/</i>||	
pula|nku#-nku#||   <i>/*those two, themselves*/</i>||	
nganaṉa|la|nku#-nku#||   <i>/*we ourselves*/</i>||	
nyura|nku#-nku#||	<i>/*you all, yourselves*/</i>||	
tjana|ya#tjana#|nku#-nku#||	<i>/*they all, themselves*/</i>||	
<h2>/*C. Now you will hear sentences with known items and others with those you are just learning.*/||</h2>
<i>/*Listen and repeat.*/</i>||	
/*1.*/|| Piti ili|tjara#-tjara# mantjila#mantjiṉi#||	
Piti ili|tjara#-tjara# mantjila#mantjiṉi# waṉintjaku#waṉinyi#|tawara#-tawara#||	

/*2.*/|| Maḻu puṉu katu tjura#tjunanyi#||	
Maḻu puṉu katu tjura#tjunanyi# papa|ngku#-ngku# ngalkuntjaku#ngalkuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*3.*/|| Mai palatja wari|ngka#-ngka# tjura#tjunanyi#||	
Mai palatja wari|ngka#-ngka# tjura#tjunanyi# uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*4.*/|| Wiltja unngu|la nyinanyi||	
Wiltja unngu|la nyinanyi puyintjaku#puyiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*5.*/|| Paluṟu|nku#-nku# ankuku#ananyi#||

/*6.*/|| Ngali|nku#-nku# ili uraṉi||

/*7.*/|| Ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# waṟu mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi#||

/*8.*/|| Nganaṉa|la#nganaṉa#|nku#-nku# wiltjaṉi||

/*9.*/|| Nyuntu|nku#-nku#|n#nyuntu# papa puwa#punganyi#||

/*10.*/|| Tjana|ya#tjana#|nku#-nku# nyinara#nyinanyi# inkanyi||

/*11.*/|| Nyura|nku#-nku# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|katingu#katinyi# ka|ya#tjana# kura|ngku#-ngku# mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi#||

/*12.*/|| Nyupali|nku#-nku# mai|ku#-ku# piti kati#katinyi#||

/*13.*/|| Punganyi pula|nku#-nku#||	

/*14.*/|| Pungu#punganyi#|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu#||

/*15.*/|| Nyangama#nyanganyi#|nku#-nku#|n#nyuntu#||

/*16.*/|| Maḻu|la|nku#-nku# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||	
<h2>/*D. Now the same sentences with their English equivalents.*/||</h2>	
/*1.*/|| Piti ili|tjara#-tjara# mantjila#mantjiṉi#||
<i>/*Get the dish with the figs*/</i>||	
Piti ili|tjara#-tjara# mantjila#mantjiṉi# waṉintjaku#waṉinyi#|tawara#-tawara#||		
<i>/*Get the dish with the figs in case it is thrown away*/</i>||	

/*2.*/|| Maḻu puṉu katu tjura#tjunanyi#||
<i>/*Put the kangaroo high in the tree*/</i>||	
Maḻu puṉu katu tjura#tjunanyi# papa|ngku#-ngku# ngalkuntjaku#ngalkuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
<i>/*Put the kangaroo high in the tree so the dog won't eat it*/</i>||	

/*3.*/|| Mai palatja wari|ngka#-ngka# tjura#tjunanyi#||
<i>/*Put that food in the cool*/</i>||	
Mai palatja wari|ngka#-ngka# tjura#tjunanyi# uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
<i>/*Put that food in the cool so it won't go bad*/</i>||	

/*4.*/|| Wiltja unngu|la nyinanyi||
<i>/*We are in the wurlie*/</i>||	
Wiltja unngu|la nyinanyi puyintjaku#puyiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
<i>/*We are in the wurlie so we won't get cold*/</i>||	

/*5.*/|| Paluṟu|nku#-nku# ankuku#ananyi#||
<i>/*He is going himself*/</i>||	

/*6.*/|| Ngali|nku#-nku# ili uraṉi||
<i>/*We (2) are collecting figs for ourselves*/</i>||	

/*7.*/|| Ngayulu|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# waṟu mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi#||
<i>/*I got wood for myself*/</i>||	

/*8.*/|| Nganaṉa|la#nganaṉa#|nku#-nku# wiltjaṉi||
<i>/*We (all) are making a wurlie for ourselves*/</i>||	

/*9.*/|| Nyuntu|nku#-nku#|n#nyuntu# papa puwa#punganyi#||
<i>/*Hit your own dog*/</i>||	

/*10.*/|| Tjana|ya#tjana#|nku#-nku# nyinara#nyinanyi# inkanyi||
<i>/*They themselves are sitting singing*/</i>||	

/*11.*/|| Nyura|nku#-nku# @ngalya-@#ngalya-#|katingu#katinyi# ka|ya#tjana# kura|ngku#-ngku# mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi#||
<i>/*You (all) brought it for yourselves and the bad ones took it*/</i>||	

/*12.*/|| Nyupali|nku#-nku# mai|ku#-ku# piti kati#katinyi#||
<i>/*You two bring your own dish for food*/</i>||	

/*13.*/|| Punganyi pula|nku#-nku#||
<i>/*They are hitting (each other) themselves (fighting)*/</i>||	

/*14.*/|| Pungu#punganyi#|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu#||
<i>/*I hit myself*/</i>||	

/*15.*/|| Nyangama#nyanganyi#|nku#-nku#|n#nyuntu#||
<i>/*Look at yourself*/</i>||	

/*16.*/|| Maḻu|la|nku#-nku# wakaṉu#wakaṉi#||
<i>/*We speared a kangaroo for ourselves*/</i>||	

<h2>/*E. Now a 4 Phase Drill.*/||</h2>
<i>/*You hear a sentence followed by a cue.*/</i>||	
<i>/*Use this cue to make a new sentence. Off you go:*/</i>||	
@Ngalya-@#ngalya-#|kati#katinyi# tjitji wiṟu, papa|ngku#-ngku# mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   uwa#unganyi#||	
@Ngalya-@#ngalya-#|uwa#unganyi# tjitji wiṟu, papa|ngku#-ngku# mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   tjura#tjunanyi#||	
@Ngalya-@#ngalya-#|tjura#tjunanyi# tjitji wiṟu, papa|ngku#-ngku# mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   waṉi#waṉinyi#||	
@Ngalya-@#ngalya-#|waṉi#waṉinyi# tjitji wiṟu, papa|ngku#-ngku# mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   witila#witiṉi#||	
@Ngalya-@#ngalya-#|witila#witiṉi# tjitji wiṟu, papa|ngku#-ngku# mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||
<i>/*Now the model changes:*/</i>||
Waḻi|ngka#-ngka#|la nyinangi#nyinanyi# ulpuru|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   tjarpangi#tjarpanyi#||
Waḻi|ngka#-ngka#|la tjarpangi#tjarpanyi# ulpuru|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   ngaringi#ngarinyi#||
Waḻi|ngka#-ngka#|la ngaringi#ngarinyi# ulpuru|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   wirkanangi#wirkananyi#||
Waḻi|ngka#-ngka#|la wirkanangi#wirkananyi# ulpuru|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   ngalkuṉingi#ngalkuṉi#||
Waḻi|ngka#-ngka#|la ngalkuṉingi#ngalkuṉi# ulpuru|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   inkangi#inkanyi#||
Waḻi|ngka#-ngka#|la inkangi#inkanyi# ulpuru|ngku#-ngku#|lanya#nganaṉa# tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||
<i>/*Now the next model:*/</i>||
Kuwari|la#nganaṉa#|nku#-nku# maḻu pauṉi uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   kuwari|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu#||
Kuwari|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# maḻu pauṉi uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   kuwari|ya#tjana#|nku#-nku#||
Kuwari|ya#tjana#|nku#-nku# maḻu pauṉi uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   kuwari|nku#-nku#|n#nyuntu#||
Kuwari|nku#-nku#|n#nyuntu# maḻu pauṉi uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   kuwari|li#ngali#|nku#-nku#||
Kuwari|li#ngali#|nku#-nku# maḻu pauṉi uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   kuwari|nku#-nku#||
Kuwari|nku#-nku# maḻu pauṉi uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||

Inkawiyangku#inkanyi#|la wantima#wantinyi# tjana kulintjaku#kulini#|tawara#-tawara#||   nyakuntjaku#nyanganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
Inkawiyangku#inkanyi#|la wantima#wantinyi# tjana nyakuntjaku#nyanganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   pitjantjaku#pitjanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Inkawiyangku#inkanyi#|la wantima#wantinyi# tjana pitjantjaku#pitjanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   tjarpantjaku#tjarpanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Inkawiyangku#inkanyi#|la wantima#wantinyi# tjana tjarpantjaku#tjarpanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   ankuntjaku#ananyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Inkawiyangku#inkanyi#|la wantima#wantinyi# tjana ankuntjaku#ananyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   wirkankuntjaku#wirkananyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Inkawiyangku#inkanyi#|la wantima#wantinyi# tjana wirkankuntjaku#wirkananyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   pungkuntjaku#punganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Inkawiyangku#inkanyi#|la wantima#wantinyi# tjana pungkuntjaku#punganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
<i>/*Now the next model:*/</i>||
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi punkantjaku#punkaṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   pungkuntjaku#punganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi pungkuntjaku#punganyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   @ma-@#ma-#|pitjantjaku#pitjanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi @ma-@#ma-#|pitjantjaku#pitjanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   @ma-@#ma-#|wirtjapakantjaku#wirtjapakaṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi @ma-@#ma-#|wirtjapakantjaku#wirtjapakaṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   wakantjaku|tawara#-tawara#||
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi wakantjaku|tawara#-tawara#||   mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   urintjaku|tawara#-tawara#||
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi urintjaku|tawara#-tawara#||   tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   witintjaku#witiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi witintjaku#witiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   puyintjaku#puyiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
Kanyiṉi|ṉa#ngayulu#|tju#ngayulu# pakaḻi puyintjaku#puyiṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
<i>/*And now the last lot of drills.*/</i>||
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# kuka katingu#katinyi# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   wiyaringkuntjaku#wiyaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# kuka katingu#katinyi# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# wiyaringkuntjaku#wiyaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||   kanyintjaku|tawara#-tawara#||
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# kuka katingu#katinyi# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# kanyintjaku|tawara#-tawara#||   pauntjaku#pauṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# kuka katingu#katinyi# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# pauntjaku#pauṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||   mungaringkuntjaku|tawara#-tawara#||
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# kuka katingu#katinyi# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# mungaringkuntjaku|tawara#-tawara#||   tjunkuntjaku#tjunanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# kuka katingu#katinyi# waḻi|kutu#-kutu# tjunkuntjaku#tjunanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||
<h2>/*F. Translate into Pitjantjatjara*/||</h2>
/*1.*/|| <i>/*The grandmother ate the food so the grandson wouldn't put it in the fire.*/</i>||	
Kami|ngku#-ngku# mai ngalkuṉu#ngalkuṉi# pakaḻi|ngku#-ngku# waṟu|ngka#-ngka# tjunkuntjaku#tjunanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*2.*/|| <i>/*They (2) ran very quickly in case the big clouds came up*/</i>||	
Wala puḻka pula wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# ngangkaḻi puḻka pakantjaku#pakaṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*3.*/|| <i>/*That poor thing is staying in the wurlie for fear that the dust will cover her*/</i>||	
Palatja ngaltutjara wiltja|ngka#-ngka# nyinanyi ulpuru|ngku#-ngku# tjutuntjaku#tjutuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*4.*/|| <i>/*The old woman is holding her dog tightly, so that it won't follow the men.*/</i>||	
Pampa|ngku#-ngku# papa puḻkaṟa witiṉi wati tjuṯa wanantjuku#wanaṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*5.*/|| <i>/*Maybe she shut her whole house in case the man who has just come goes in*/</i>||	
Tjinguṟu paluṟu|ngku#-ngku# waḻi uwankara patiṉu#patiṉi# wati kuwari wirkankuntja#wirkananyi# tjarpantjaku#tjarpanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*6.*/|| <i>/*The women always only take one in case they are finished up*/</i>||	
Minyma tjuṯa|ngku#-ngku# titutjara|ngku#-ngku# kutju mantjilpai#mantjiṉi# wiyaringkuntjaku#wiyaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||	
	
/*7.*/|| <i>/*The man covered the shot dog with earth and stones too for fear of stench*/</i>||
Wati|ngku#-ngku# papa pauntja#pauṉi# paṉa|ngka#-ngka# tjutuṉu#tjutuṉi#, apu|ngka#-ngka# kuḻu, uṉaringkuntjaku#uṉaringanyi#|tawara#-tawara#||

/*8.*/|| <i>/*The child the spilt food and put it in a dish, so that dogs wouldn't eat it.*/</i>||
Tjitji|ngku#-ngku# mai punkantja#punkaṉi# uraṟa#uraṉi# tjunu#tjunanyi# piti|ngka#-ngka#, papa|ngku#-ngku# ngalkuntjaku#ngalkuṉi#|tawara#-tawara#||

<i>/*End of Unit 27*/</i>||

<h2>/*B. Text*/||</h2>
<b>Kami|ṟara#-ṟara# Pula Iili|ngka#-ngka# Nyinantja#nyinanyi#</b>||	
<i>/*Grandmother and Grandson in the Rain*/</i>||	
Palu ngula kunyu nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# watjaṉu#watjaṉi# nyaa, ngalta tjukutjuku, munu kunyu kalkuṟa#kalkuṉi# ankula#ananyi# tjuṯa mantjiṉu#mantjiṉi# munu wantikatingu#wantikatinyi# kami|ngku#-ngku# ngula mai nyara palunya#paluṟu# mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#, munu kunyu pitjala#pitjanyi# watjaṉu#watjaṉi# "Kami, ngalta|ṉa#ngayulu# parari nguwanpa nyakula#nyinanyi# wantikatingu#wantikatinyi#".|| Ka watjaṉu#watjaṉi#, "Yaaltji?"|| Ka watjaṉu#watjaṉi# "Ila nguwanpa.|| Tjinguṟu nyuntu ankula#ananyi# tjawaṟa#tjawaṉi# mai mantjilku#mantjiṉi# paṉa|ngka#-ngka# unngu|nguṟu#-nguṟu#".|| Ka kunyu kulinu#kulini# munu watjaṉu#watjaṉi#, "Mungawinki|ṉa#ngayulu# ananyi".|| Palu mungawinki kami pakaṉu#pakaṉi#, ka kunyu nyiiṉka anu#ananyi# ngura|nguṟu#-nguṟu# munu ankula#ananyi# kumpiṟa#kumpiri# ngaṟangi#ngaṟanyi# minyma panya ankuntjaku#ananyi#.|| Ka minyma anu#ananyi# ka nyiiṉka panya pitjangu#pitjanyi# ngura|kutu#-kutu# munu waṟu puḻkaṟa ngantjiningi#ngantjini# munu untjunarira#untjunarinyi# tjulpu tjukutjuku, wiṟatju pungu#punganyi#, munu kuliningi#kulini#, "Yaaltjingalku|ṉa#ngayulu#?"|| Munu panya kulira#kulini# kulira#kulini# tjulpu panya wamulu nyaaṉu munu|nku#-nku# uwankara walkatjunu#walkatjunanyi# wamulu|ngka#-ngka# munu kunyu kuṟu|ngku#-ngku# puṯu nyangangi#nyanganyi#, unngu kutju uwankara, munu paṯaṟa#paṯaṉi# nyinangi#nyinanyi# kami|ku#-ku#, panya kami|ku#-ku# ngura|nguṟu#-nguṟu#.|| Ka kunyu kami panya|ngku#-ngku# rawa|ngku#-ngku# tjawaṟa#tjawaṉi# tjawaṟa#tjawaṉi# mai uraṟa#uraṉi# uraṟa#uraṉi# katingu#katinyi# ngura|kutu#-kutu#.|| Ka wiltja|nguṟu#-nguṟu# nyirkingi#nyirkinyi#, ka kunyu puḻkaṟa nguḻuringu#nguḻuringanyi# mamu palku kulira#kulini#, munu maḻaku anu#ananyi# munu ngaṟala#ngaṟanyi# kuliningi#kulini# "Nyaa panyatja?"|| Ka kunyu piṟuku wiltja kutjupa|nguṟu#-nguṟu# wirkanu#wirkananyi# munu kunyu nyangangi#nyanganyi#, rawa|ngku#-ngku# kunyu nyangangi#nyanganyi# ka kunyu wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi# munu ngaṟala#ngaṟanyi# pitjangu#pitjanyi# palu ilaringkula#ilaringanyi# kunyu piṟuku nyangangi#nyanganyi# - kuṟu|ngku#-ngku# nyakuwiya#nyanganyi# panya wamulu tjuṯa|tjara#-tjara# munu kunyu rawa|ngku#-ngku# nyangangi#nyanganyi# ka kunyu nguḻu wirtjapakaṉingi#wirtjapakaṉi#.|| Ka kami kunyu mina|ngku#-ngku# puyiṉu#puyiṉi# ka kunyu puḻkaṟa tjititingangi#tjititinganyi# munu uparingu#uparinganyi#, minyma panya.|| Ka kutjupa, maḻa mulapa @para-@#para-#|nyirkingi#nyirkinyi# ka kunyu minyma panya parari punkaṉu#punkaṉi# munu ilungu#ilunyi#.||

<h2>/*D. Questions*/||</h2>	
/*1.*/|| Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# ankula#ananyi# nyaa nyakula#nyinanyi# wantikatingu#wantikatinyi# kami|ku#-ku#?||	
Mai ngalta wantikatingu#wantikatinyi# kami|ngku#-ngku# @ma-@#ma-#|pitjala#pitjanyi# mantjintjaku#mantjiṉi#.||
Nyiiṉka|ngku#-ngku# ankula#ananyi# nyaa nyakula#nyinanyi# wantikatingu#wantikatinyi# kami|ku#-ku#?||

/*2.*/|| Nyaaku paluṟu parari nguwanpa wantikatingu#wantikatinyi#?||	
Parari nguwanpa wantikatingu#wantikatinyi# kami ngura|nguṟu#-nguṟu# ankuntjaku#ananyi#.||
Nyaaku paluṟu parari nguwanpa wantikatingu#wantikatinyi#?||	

/*3.*/|| Mungawinki, kami pakanyangka#pakaṉi# nyiiṉka|ngu#-ngku#|nku#-nku# nyaaṉu?||	
Paluṟu|nku#-nku# walkatjunu#walkatjunanyi# wamulu|ngka#-ngka#.||
Mungawinki, kami pakanyangka#pakaṉi# nyiiṉka|ngu#-ngku#|nku#-nku# nyaaṉu?||	

/*4.*/|| Ka kami|ngku#-ngku#, mai|tjara#-tjara# pitjala#pitjanyi#, nyaa palku nyangu#nyanganyi#?||	
Kami|ngku#-ngku# mamu palku nyangu#nyanganyi# wiltja|nguṟu#-nguṟu# nyirkinyangka#nyirkinyi#.||
Ka kami|ngku#-ngku#, mai|tjara#-tjara# pitjala#pitjanyi#, nyaa palku nyangu#nyanganyi#?||	

/*5.*/|| Munu nyaaṉu kami?||
Nguḻu mulapa @ma-@#ma-#|wirtjapakaṉu#wirtjapakaṉi#.||
Munu nyaaṉu kami?||

/*6.*/|| Ngaltutjara, nyaaringu#nyaaringanyi# uṟil|ta#-ta# nguḻu rawa nyinara#nyinanyi#?||	
Uparingu#uparinganyi# paluṟu, munu ilungu#ilunyi#.||
Ngaltutjara, nyaaringu#nyaaringanyi# uṟil|ta#-ta# nguḻu rawa nyinara#nyinanyi#?||
